Sichuan's public opinion is being hijacked by warlords, making it difficult for them to express their true feelings to the central government. It is hoped that the national public opinion circles can create true public opinion on the Sichuan situation and severely sanction it with the central force of public opinion, so that all parties will be aware and vigilant. He will send a telegram to the Sichuan generals in his personal name to respect the prestige of the central government and abide by the 17-year decree governing Sichuan, striving to implement it and stating that local disputes should be resolved locally or resolved by the power of the central government. It is impossible for the central government to send people to mediate. (30th Special Dispatch) (Nanjing) A certain organization received a telegram from Sichuan, in which Tian Songyao denied having jointly issued a telegram with Deng Xihou and Liu Wenhui to cooperate among the three forces. Hopes for a peaceful resolution of the Sichuan situation remain slim. (30th Special Dispatch) (Nanjing) He Yingqin said that the Sichuan situation is not optimistic and that the central government should take effective measures to stop it. Rumors that a Sichuan Post-Settlement Committee will be established, with Zhang Qun as the chairman, are untrue. (30th Special Dispatch) (Chengdu) Liu Xiang has been sending telegrams for days, urging Deng Xihou to send troops to attack Liu Wenhui. Otherwise, he should withdraw from Jianyang and Ziyang within three days, so that the 20th Army can advance westward. Deng was very angry upon receiving the telegram. The cooperation between the three forces is becoming more resolute. Deng told people that in the current situation, it is impossible to survive without joining hands with Tian and Liu. He has telegraphed the troops stationed in Jianzi to prepare for resistance and, if necessary, can transfer two divisions to be commanded by Army Commander Liu (Wenhui). (30th Central News Agency dispatch) (Hankou) Wang Fangzhou's mission this time, acting on the orders of Liu Xiang, to visit Chiang Kaishek in Hankou is threefold: (1) to present to Chiang the distress of using troops this time and seek understanding; (2) to declare that the 20th Army has the certainty of unifying Sichuan and ask Chiang to trust them; and (3) to represent the 20th Army generals in opposing the establishment of the Sichuan Provincial Government Reorganization Committee and rejecting the entry of a certain person into Sichuan. Central Broadcasting Station

Announces the Truth About the Secret Document of the Japanese Ministry of Colonial Affairs 33

Points Out Policy of Using Chinese to Control Chinese, Confirms the Despicable Tactics of the Japanese (Nanjing) At 6:30 tonight, the Central Broadcasting Station used Japanese to announce to the Japanese people the contents of the secret document of the Japanese Ministry of Colonial Affairs, refuting Matsuoka's accusation that it was a forgery. It stated that the secret document was obtained by a lawyer in Harbin from a Japanese person he had bought off. The origin of the document is very clear and is definitely not a forgery by the Chinese. One section of the resolution stated that it is necessary to imitate the Chinese policy of using barbarians to control barbarians, and Japan should adopt a policy of using Chinese to control Chinese. According to Japanese foreign policy since the Republic of China, it has consistently used divisive tactics, utilizing Chinese to kill Chinese and promoting warlord infighting, while the Japanese reap the benefits. This is consistent with the resolution and confirms the despicable tactics of the Japanese. (30th China United Press dispatch)

Han Fuqu

Discusses Local Administration in Western Shandong 34

Pingyin County Magistrate and Others Dismissed. Han Fuqu of Jinan discussed that during his inspection of the four counties, Changqing was generally better. I will go to Jiaodong to inspect the student unrest after Liu Zhennian's troops have completely left Shandong. There is nothing significant about the student unrest, but the joint examinations are an order from the Ministry of Education. Since they are students, they cannot oppose the examinations. If they can obey the order and take the joint examinations, they can be ordered to return to school. Detailed measures need to be stipulated by the Education Department. Britain Deals with War Debts with a Combination of Firmness and Flexibility 55

〓Reply to the US Note Ready for Dispatch〓

Content States Reasons for Requesting Deferment to Maintain World Trust, Indicates Readiness to Pay in Cash if the US Insists on Debt Repayment at Maturity ▲Havas, London, 29th - The British government's response to the American note seems to be completely drafted. Tonight, Prime Minister MacDonald had an audience with the King for over an hour to discuss the British debt issue. Political figures generally believe that this reply is one of the most important documents Britain has sent to a foreign country in many years. In terms of its content, the reply not only explains Britain's financial position but also carries extremely important political significance, as seen in the Prime Minister's special audience with the King for this matter. ▲National News Agency, London, 30th - It is reported that after the British government convened a cabinet meeting to discuss war debts, it decided that if the United States insists on payment of the installment due on December 15, Britain is prepared to pay it. According to the Daily Mail, the Bank of England has already followed the Ministry of Finance's order to arrange the transfer of 30 million pounds to New York to prepare for debt repayment. The first batch of 3 million pounds is scheduled to depart today, with the remainder to be shipped in batches. The British government's reply to the US State Department is expected to be sent out today. The content will state that if the United States insists on payment, Britain will comply without delay. However, it will also state in the strongest terms that the British government firmly believes that a deferment is necessary to maintain world confidence. Furthermore, it will solemnly state other payment methods, hoping that by demonstrating the British government's ability to pay and explaining the strong reasons for the need for deferment, it can convince the United States that the installment does not necessarily need to be paid on schedule. Additionally, it is reported that the reply will hint that a deferment would have a more stabilizing effect on the economy than paying on schedule.

▲Reuters, London, 29th - British cabinet members are still intently drafting the reply to the United States regarding war debts. MacDonald, Baldwin, Chamberlain, Simon, Hore-Belisha, and others all met today on Downing Street. The British Ambassador to France, Lord Tyrrell, returned to London last night and met with the Prime Minister for 45 minutes before also going to the Foreign Office to deliberate. It is expected that the draft reply can be submitted to the weekly cabinet meeting tomorrow. The entire issue of war debt deferment hinges on whether the reasons given in the reply are sufficient and how these reasons are presented. Therefore, the careful consideration of the draft reply is taking considerable time and effort. In the afternoon, the Prime Minister had an audience with the King, reportedly discussing the war debt issue. Tonight, the cabinet met in the House of Commons for a short period, also in connection with the reply to the United States. They will meet again tomorrow morning. It is expected that this reply, while limited to stating reasons for reconsidering the war debts and deferring the December installment, must provide detailed reasons and support them with accurate and irrefutable facts. The reply will mention the impact of the Lausanne reparations agreement to demonstrate that Britain may not be able to continue paying US debts when European countries are not repaying their debts to Britain. Britain has already paid more to the United States than it has received from its debtor nations by 200 million pounds. If comparing the original debt figures, other countries owe Britain more than Britain owes the United States.

Current Commentary

General Mobilization for National Salvation Through Entertainment 61

After initiating the monthly donation campaign to relieve Northeastern refugees and aid the Northeastern volunteer armies, some are now shouting the slogan of "General Mobilization for National Salvation Through Entertainment" and launching a charity performance for Northeastern refugees. While this may be one way to save the nation, further thought makes this phenomenon truly disheartening. The cry for "National Salvation" didn't start today. Around the time of the September 18th Incident and the January 28th Incident, nearly every citizen of the Republic of China wept and cried out in anguish, with mouths speaking of "National Salvation" and pens writing about "National Salvation." The calls for "Recovering Lost Territory by Force" and "Long-Term Resistance" were even more persistent. However, now, just one year later, even these empty cries have faded and disappeared with the passing of time. What is starkly presented before our eyes is the fact that a puppet regime has been established outside the customs, the Zhabei-Wusong area has become a painful picture of shattered tiles and ruined walls, and there are also the tragic bloody footprints of the Northeastern volunteer armies' arduous struggle and the sorrowful cries of the Northeastern refugees who have become slaves before death. The cold wind has risen, and winter has arrived. All the "masters," "madams," "young masters," and "modern ladies" have already put on warm winter clothes and prepared luxurious furs, electric heaters, champagne, and the like, waiting for the "auspicious snow" to arrive so they can leisurely enjoy the pleasure of "warming wine around the stove" or "visiting plum blossoms in the snow." But what about the Northeastern volunteer armies? Under the early cold of the icy and snowy wilderness, they only have thin clothes dancing in the north wind, only cold iron, only arduous and tragic hunger, only heroic struggle, only blood scattered across the white mountains and black waters, and great sacrifices. In comparison, we cannot but admit that the bodies of the "masters," "madams," "young masters," and "ladies" are too warm, while the Northeastern volunteer armies are too cold. Conversely, we cannot but admit that the hearts of the "masters," "madams," "young masters," and "ladies" are too cold, while every member of the Northeastern volunteer armies has a heart filled with heat. What are the Northeastern volunteer armies fighting arduously for? What are the Northeastern refugees wandering around for? It is for the survival of our nation, for resisting violence, and for upholding justice and righteousness. Then, is their freezing and hunger justified? Conversely, is our warmth, fullness, and enjoyment justified? If not, then what should we do? Here, each of us should bury our heads in contemplation, assuming that we have not yet become insensitive wood or stone. From "shouting for recovering lost territory by force" to "silent and soundless," from "silent and soundless" to "National Salvation Through Entertainment," is this comical or tragic? Look at how the invading countries do what they say, achieving what they set out to do, without empty slogans or pointless tears. Even when society and the economy are declining and collapsing, their people still enthusiastically donate to the country for the sake of aggression. What about us? Shouldn't we be even more willing to contribute our strength if we have strength and donate money if we have money, for the sake of self-defense and for the sake of fighting for the survival of our nation? Now, let us change the slogan of "recovering lost territory by force" to "National Salvation Through Entertainment" and let everyone have a bitter smile through tears. But young masters and ladies, this time, I hope you are also enthusiastic and active. Because whether it is a tearful smile or a joyful smile, you will have completed the task of "National Salvation Through Entertainment," and the Northeastern refugees and volunteer armies will also receive your great gift. Now, let us shout for "National Salvation Through Entertainment!" Young masters and ladies, are you willing to come and appreciate this entertainment filled with blood and tears for "National Salvation?"

France and Russia

Non-Aggression Treaty Established 62

▲Reuters, Paris, 29th - The Franco-Russian non-aggression treaty was signed today at the French Foreign Ministry by French Premier Herriot and Russian Ambassador to France Dovgalevsky. The French Premier then spoke, saying that he extended his respects to the Soviet Russian people and that France was willing to enhance mutual trust with them. With the establishment of this treaty, the system of non-aggression pacts is now complete and should help consolidate peace. The Russian Ambassador replied that the Soviet Union attached great importance to the political and moral value of this treaty, which has proven France and Russia's desire for peace.

▲Havas, Paris, 29th - The French Foreign Ministry announced that the French government and Russia have concluded a mutual non-aggression treaty. What should be stated at the time of signing is that no clause of the treaty restricts the content of future Russo-French economic agreements or the French government's complete freedom regarding tariffs. Treaty Full text of the Treaty of Non-Aggression between France and the Soviet Union The full text is as follows: The Central Executive Committee of the Soviet Union and the President of the French Republic, in order to consolidate peace, promote friendship between the two sides, and demonstrate the peaceful intentions extended by the Anti-War Pact of August 27, 1928, in the spirit of fulfilling past international responsibilities, have concluded the following agreement: [Article 1] Neither party shall, alone or in conjunction with another country, attack the other party from the sea, land, or air, and shall respect the sovereignty of the other party's territory and possessions. [Article 2] If either party is attacked by another country or countries, the other party shall not provide direct or indirect assistance to the attackers. If one party actively attacks a third country, the other party may terminate the present treaty with notice. [Article 3] The above two articles do not overturn or change the rights acquired by both parties in the various treaties concluded before this treaty, but both parties simultaneously declare that they are not bound by any provision in any previous treaty that requires participation in an attack by a third party. [Article 4] Neither party may participate in any international agreement that restricts the other party's trade and financing, or any measures that prevent the other party's foreign trade. [Article 5] Both parties shall respect the sovereignty of the other party's territory and possessions in accordance with the first article of the agreement, and shall not interfere in the other party's internal affairs, specifically, shall not engage in any direct actions, instigating or encouraging any disturbances, propaganda, or attempts to interfere, in order to undermine the other party's territorial integrity, or to change the other party's political and social system in whole or in part by force. Both parties shall also not initiate, support, supply, subsidize, or permit military organizations in their respective countries to attack the other party's territory or overthrow the other party's government by force. [Article 6] Stipulates that all conflicts and disputes between the two parties should be resolved by peaceful means, as pointed out in the simultaneously concluded mediation agreement. [Article 7] Stipulates that the French and Russian texts of the agreement are equally valid, and the agreement shall take effect only after the exchange of ratification documents in Moscow. The agreement may not be terminated within two years after its implementation. Thereafter, if either party wishes to terminate the agreement, it must notify the other party one year in advance.

Attached Mediation Agreement The Franco-Russian Mediation Agreement has eight articles. Its content stipulates that from the effective date of the agreement, any dispute between the two parties that cannot be resolved through diplomatic means must be submitted to a mediation committee. The committee shall be composed of two representatives appointed by each of the two governments, and its chairman must be a national of the country where the meeting is held. Experts may also be hired to participate in the committee in a consultative capacity, and witnesses may also participate when necessary. The committee members shall convene once a year, but both parties may agree to postpone it to the following year. In case of urgent need, a temporary meeting may be requested. Fifteen days before the meeting, both parties must submit a list of the issues to be discussed through diplomatic procedures. The meeting time is limited to fifteen days, but it can be extended with the consent of both parties. The meeting address shall alternate between Paris and Moscow. In addition, it is stipulated that the committee meeting is only valid if all members of both parties are present, and the resolution must be passed unanimously. If a unanimous vote cannot be obtained, either party may request a special meeting within four months of the closing of the meeting to resolve the matter. Both parties must respond within three months as to whether or not they approve of the committee's proposals regarding mediation procedures. Finally, the effective period of the agreement is the same as that of the non-aggression treaty listed above. (TASS dispatch)

Japanese Army in the Korean Border

Digging Trenches and Laying Electric Fences 63

Adding 500 Armed Police to Guard Against Korean Independence Party Crossing the Border ▲Hualian News Agency, Seoul, 3rd - Since September 18th, the Korean Government-General has seen an increase in the activity of the Korean Independence Party and the Korean Communist Party, frequently disrupting the passage of military trains. It is reported that this plan has been approved by the Colonial Affairs Ministry and will be implemented soon. According to reports, Korean farmers' lives are becoming increasingly impoverished, and with the oppression of Japanese imperialism worsening, the number of people automatically participating in the revolutionary movement is increasing daily, leaving the proponents of militarism powerless.

Anti-Jewish Wave in Poland 64

▲National News Agency, Warsaw, 29th - An anti-Jewish wave suddenly broke out in Lviv, Poland today. The initial cause was that a Jewish student killed a Polish student in a fight. Polish students were greatly angered, and many civilians expressed sympathy for the Polish student, so they held demonstrations in the streets. The windows of shops set up by Jews were destroyed, and Jews walking on the road were beaten, even women were not spared. When the police heard the news, they rushed to the scene, and more than eighty people on both sides were injured. The current government authorities strictly prohibit the dissemination of news about the riots, and four newspapers have been suspended indefinitely for publishing the news. The Polish capital has obviously been affected by this wave, because Polish students at the University of Warsaw intend to expel Jewish students from the school, and the president has temporarily closed the school to prevent the spread of the wave.

Starving Marchers Approaching Washington D.C. 67

▲National News Agency, Washington D.C., 29th - The leaders of the American starvation marchers arrived in Washington D.C. today, requesting permission for the marchers to enter the city and provide accommodation and food for the first three days of next week. Japanese Budget Contradictions - Japanese Dispatch 68

[Even if the whole country turns to scorched earth, we must persist in our claims to Manchuria...] This is Japan amidst tense international relations. One aspect of its foreign policy reveals Japan's true intentions more openly, and we can also see where all its conspiracies lie.

Originally, after the assassination of Prime Minister Tsuyoshi Inukai on May 15th of this year, parliamentary politics in Japan were fundamentally shaken. The liberalism advocated by the two major opposing parties was not only powerless but also declining. To put it more bluntly, militarism was on the rise, virtually overriding the appointed constitution. However, they could still explain that Japan's constitutional politics were not democratic but monarchical, and that the cabinet was not entirely responsible to the parliament but to the Emperor. The cabinet of Prime Minister Saitō Makoto was called a "cooperative cabinet." At the beginning of its formation, it originally intended to bring together various factions, at least the outstanding members of the two major parties, the Seiyūkai and the Minseitō, to serve as cabinet members, forming a so-called "cabinet of talent." However, in reality, most Japanese people considered this only a cabinet of second-rate talent. Nevertheless, with a few ministers and vice-ministers from both the Seiyūkai and Minseitō as political officials, the cabinet from the beginning included the army, navy, and two not-very-harmonious political parties merged together. They themselves called it a "cooperative cabinet," but in reality, it was a mixed cabinet. In the Saitō cabinet, there was the Japanese-style fascist tendency of the military, the landlords and Mitsui affiliated members of the Seiyūkai, and the liberalism and Mitsubishi affiliated members of the Minseitō. Within the military, there was also competition between the army and navy, and within the army, there was a distinction between gradualists and radicals. Therefore, the Saitō cabinet was in a state of uncertainty from the beginning. From June to now, it has been half a year, and the Saitō cabinet is considered long-lived. Its biggest difficulty at present is that when the budget was being drafted, the so-called "national defense enhancement," "military equipment improvement," "Manchurian Incident" expenses, "situation relief" funds, plus the new demands of various ministries and agencies, had already exceeded 1.4 billion yen. If all were approved, plus all the regular expenses, then the total budget for the next year would be 3 billion yen, while the total revenue would be at most 1.286 billion yen. Given the current state of the national economy, how could it bear this burden? Moreover, when will the Manchurian problem be resolved? How long will the [Manchurian Incident expenses] continue, and when will it come to an end? No one can predict. This means that before Japan earns any money, it will have to subsidize at least 132 million yen in military expenses every year. After a modification, the army and finance ministries caused countless troubles, almost causing the cabinet to collapse. After much mediation, a special increase of 95 million yen was given to the military, temporarily patching up the current rift. The 1933 budget, totaling 2.238 billion yen in expenditure, is the largest budget in Japan's history. The average burden per person is 31 yen. Such a huge budget is considered by financial and political circles in Japan to be a crisis that could lead Japan's finances to bankruptcy. However, the military authorities argue that this is an emergency and that such a huge budget is necessary. This budget has two unprecedented features: first, the deficit is entirely filled by public bonds; second, the military expenditure has increased enormously. In the 1933 Japanese budget, the national treasury's regular revenue is only 1.288 billion yen, and even with temporary revenue, it is only 1.341 billion yen. The difference is still 900 million yen, and there is no other way to increase revenue to fill the gap. Therefore, the public bonds currently planned to be issued, such as the Manchurian Incident expenses, civil engineering projects, telephone projects, earthquake relief bonds, military improvement expenses, etc., all new budgets, must be filled by public bonds. The number of issued bonds must be at least 896 million yen, accounting for 40% of the total expenditure. However, among its regular national tax revenue, tax revenue is 691 million yen, state property revenue is 457 million yen, and stamp tax revenue is 67 million yen. Compared with the tax revenue three or four years ago, it has decreased from over 900 million to 690 million yen (the decline in tax revenue shows the general pain of the Japanese situation). Comparing tax revenue with expenditure, it is only 30% of the total, even less than one-tenth of the public bonds. The rapid increase in military expenditure is also the current cancer of the Japanese budget. Especially in the last two years, it has increased rapidly and significantly. According to its military, the explanation is due to the outbreak of the Manchurian Incident. The army and navy together total 820 million yen. Even if all the tax revenue is used for military expenses, it is still 130 million yen short. Comparing military expenditure with total expenditure, it actually accounts for 36%. It is strongly remembered that between 1919 and 1922, Japanese military expenditure accounted for 42% to 49% of the total expenditure. At that time, it was appropriate after the European War and during the military period of the Siberian Expedition, so military expenditure increased extraordinarily. However, at that time, Japan made a fortune of over 10 billion during the war, and the national economic power was indeed much stronger than it is now. The total budget expenditure was only 1.6 billion. From 1930, military expenditure began to decrease (at that time, preparations were being made to restore the gold standard), but it increased sharply last year, from 27% the previous year to 35%, and it will strongly increase to 36% next year. This does not include temporary expenses such as troop increases in the Northeast. Although it is less than the 80% of military expenditure during the Russo-Japanese War, it is still a kind of budget that must be increased during the final account. Although it has been roughly determined on the surface, the Seiyūkai's Mitsuchi Tetsuzo and the Minseitō's Yamamoto, the Home Minister, are in a period of fierce fighting, from secret struggles to open brawls, for the civil engineering construction plan. The details will be reported later. (Tokyo, November 25th)

▲ Restoring Armories and Building Steel Mills

▲ Issuing Public Bonds is Also a New Puppet Show

A dispatch from Beiping states that the Japanese army in the Northeast is, on the one hand, fighting in various places, vainly hoping to extinguish the righteous army's forces, and on the other hand, establishing its own political, economic, and military forces. Recently, in order to utilize the machinery of the armories in the three eastern provinces to manufacture weapons, it negotiated with the various puppets of the puppet state and decided to start work in mid-March of next spring, naming it the [Fengtian Arsenal Co., Ltd.], directly under the jurisdiction of the Japanese Kwantung Army Headquarters. The capital is 80 million yuan, with the puppet state government investing 40 million yuan in fixed capital and the Japanese side investing 40 million yuan in working capital. It is reported that the factory buildings, offices, and warehouses of the armory, aviation department, and mortar factory will be assigned to the arsenal, with the factory site extending from Shanzuizi in the east to Huanggu Tun in the west, Ertaizi in the north, and Dananguan in the south. All the factory buildings within it will be used. It is reported that Lieutenant Colonel Yoshikawa has been internally appointed as the factory director, and Majors Amano and Hiraki as deputy factory directors. 1,500 workers will be employed. In addition to rifles and artillery shells, the output can produce 150 to 200 light machine guns, 3 to 6 75mm cannons, 12 to 20 armored vehicles, 3 to 7 tanks, and 40 to 70 cars per month. It is reported that the machinery in each factory only restores one-fifth of the rifle factory, one-thirtieth of the artillery shell factory, one-tenth of the pharmaceutical factory, one-third of the power plant, and one-fifth of the waterworks and steam plant. In the future, when the Japanese side considers it smooth, it will fully restore them and can manufacture guns and cannons themselves. This is not only a symbol of suppressing the righteous army but also of destroying peace in East Asia, because once the machinery in the factory is modified, it can manufacture poison gas and other new weapons. The activities of Japanese soldiers are also very severe. Those who came to the Northeast this month to inspect include Major General Nagata, the Second Department Chief of the Japanese General Staff Headquarters, Director Honto, and Secretary Toyo, as well as Regiment Commander Tamon (the first to revolt during the Pan Incident). On the 11th, he went to the eastern border to supervise the army. Recently, the Shenyang County Public Security Bureau ordered each district to carry out suppression of guerrillas. The puppet state government has recently been in extreme poverty and has decided to issue so-called national construction bonds to alleviate the immediate crisis. The fixed amount of the issue is 30 million yuan, with a term of 20 years and an interest rate of 5%, scheduled to be sold in mid-December. However, at this time when people's livelihoods are in dire straits, the people are naturally unable to buy them, and they will be bought by the Japanese, causing the Japanese economic power to extend into the political system. Before March, the Japanese zaibatsu Mitsui once planned to lend 30 million yuan to the puppet state, but it was abandoned for other reasons. Today, the puppet state is issuing 30 million yuan in public bonds, echoing each other before and after, showing that this is another puppet show performed by the Japanese and Chinese traitors. Recently, the Japanese side has also decided to promote the establishment of the Showa Steel Works with a capital of 33 million yen, chaired by Mantetsu's Director Godo. This matter has attracted great attention from all parties because the steel mill is a major steel plant pre-planned by Japan in East Asia, and its military significance is very important.

The Situation in the Sichuan War Changes Again 71

▲ Liu Wenhui's Troops Withdraw from Luzhou and Attack Deng and Tian

▲ But at the Same Time, There are Rumors of a Re-organization of the Baoding Faction

A dispatch from Chongqing states that the Sichuan war, which broke out in the Shunqing area of the north on October 2nd and spread to the east, south, and Chengdu areas, has lasted for nearly two months to this day. According to recent news from various sources and observations of the situation, it has begun to show a tendency to end, but there are still major changes brewing in secret, and the future of the Sichuan situation is still difficult to be optimistic about. The details are as follows: (The bloody battle between the Allied Army and Liu Wenhui) After the conflict between the 24th Army, stationed by Liu Wenhui, and the 23rd Division of Luo Zezhou, stationed in Wusheng, on October 2nd, the Allied Army group was formed. Liu Xiang of the 21st Army, Deng Xihou of the 28th Army, Tian Songyao of the 29th Army, Yang Sen of the 20th Army, Liu Chenghou, the Border Defense Commissioner of Sichuan and Shaanxi, Luo Zezhou of the 23rd Division, and Li Jiayu of the New 6th Division united and jointly opposed the 24th Army. In the northern part of Sichuan, the Allied forces of Li, Luo, Yang, Liu, and Tian launched an attack on the 24th Army. Starting on October 16th, the Allied forces captured Shunqing, Suining, Pengxi, Anyue, and Lezhi of the 24th Army. On November 18th, they attacked Zizhong. Li and Yang fought a bloody battle with Liu Wenhui's troops for three days, engaging in more than ten hand-to-hand combats, before finally capturing Zizhong. It is estimated that the deaths on both sides exceeded a thousand. They then occupied Jianyang. In the southeastern area, Liu Xiang officially fought against the 24th Army on October 21st, and successively occupied Tongnan, Dazu, Yongchuan, Rongchang, Longchang, Jiangjin, and Hejiang, and launched a general attack on Luzhou. The 24th Army dispatched five brigades to defend Luzhou. The two sides held each other for more than half a month, with deaths exceeding 5,000. On the 22nd, Liu Xiang's troops finally captured Luzhou, and then occupied Gulan, Nanxi, Jiang'an, Songxian, Neijiang, Fushun, Rongxian, Yuyuan, Xufu, Naxi, and Yangxian. On November 16th, Tian Songyao and Deng Xihou jointly attacked the 24th Army in Chengdu, engaging in street battles. The two sides held each other for three days, with the total number of deaths exceeding 8,000. The 28th Army had occupied Renshou, Chongqing, and Shuangliu. (The Allied Army Ceases Fire but the Fighting in Chengdu Continues) After capturing Luxian, Xufu, and Rongxian, Liu Xiang of the 21st Army stopped advancing. The vanguard of the Liu army is currently holding a position against the 24th Army in the Jiading area, but neither side has opened fire. Yang Sen and Li Qixiang also stopped military action after capturing Zizhong and Jianyang and convened a meeting of generals in Jianyang to discuss the aftermath of the Sichuan situation. On the surface, the Sichuan war seems to have come to an end and there is hope for a resolution, but the fighting in the Chengdu area is still fierce. Deng, Tian, and Liu are fighting to the death. Before the Sichuan war, Liu Wenhui tried his best to win over Deng Xihou, wanting him to help him protect his strength and was willing to offer Renshou, Shuangliu, and Chongqing, and send 2 million yuan in military expenses. But Tian's army pressed Liu very hard, and Deng Xihou not only did not cover Liu's army but also sided with Tian's army, which angered Liu Wenhui. He then ordered all the troops guarding Luxian to withdraw and completely allow the 21st Army to occupy the counties below Jiading. He then concentrated his strength in Chengdu, fiercely attacking the 28th and 29th armies, to protect his interests in the Chengdu area and the empty title of provincial chairman (because Chengdu is the capital of Sichuan province, if Liu abandons it),

the title of chairman will have nothing to attach to). It is estimated that the 24th Army in Chengdu has more than 450 companies. Recently, the Kangchuan army has also been successively transferred back to reinforce Chengdu. The armory of the 29th Army in Chengdu has been occupied by the 24th Army. The headquarters of the 29th Army has been moved to Santai, and the headquarters of the 28th Army has been moved to Hanzhou. The two armies are near Fengshan, 15 miles away from Chengdu, and Chengdu is completely in the hands of the 24th Army. (There is hope for the Baoding faction to reorganize) After the 28th Army withdrew from Chengdu, the army commander Deng Xihou issued a telegram on the 19th, advocating a unanimous ceasefire and peace talks. The second-level generals of the 24th, 28th, and 29th armies all sent telegrams in support, advocating that a Sichuan situation aftermath meeting be held in Zizhong or Suining to jointly discuss and manage Sichuan according to the outline of the Sichuan administration draft of the former 96 generals. At the same time, Xiang Yuren, the deputy commander of the 24th Army, also loudly called for the reorganization of the Baoding faction generals (among the military officers in Sichuan, there are three factions: Baoding,

Quick Training, and Military Officer. Deng Xihou, Tian Songyao, and Liu Wenhui are from the Baoding faction, Liu Xiang and Yang Sen are from the Quick Training faction, and Li Qixiang and Luo Zezhou are from the Military Officer faction. The second-level generals of each army are also mostly from these three factions). They are now separately communicating with Tian and Deng, actively carrying out this plan. Tian and Deng also have the intention of supporting it. New changes are brewing, but they have not yet been revealed on the surface. (November 26th)

Inside Story of the Change in the Guizhou Situation 72

▲ Mao Guangxiang and Wang Jialie Compete for Power

▲ The Background is Related to the Two Lius in Sichuan

A dispatch from Chongqing states that while the Sichuan war has not yet ended, the Guizhou province has also been heard to have a civil war. In recent days, guns and cannons have been firing on the Wujiang River, and Mao (Guangxiang) and Wang (Jialie) have actually engaged in fighting, which has had a considerable impact on the Sichuan situation and a new change is occurring. Retracing the situation in Guizhou since the death of Zhou Xicheng, Mao Guangxiang took over the military and civilian affairs. For the past two years, it has been quite peaceful, but Wang Jialie, who was guarding the Hongjiang area, due to his sufficient strength and great momentum, urgently wanted to realize his ambition to become the chairman, so he led his troops back to Guizhou, forcing Mao to step down. Seeing Wang's strength, Mao did not dare to compete with him, so he swallowed his anger and handed over both the position of commander of the 25th Army and the chairman of the Guizhou Provincial Government to Wang, while he only held the title of commander-in-chief of the 18th Route Army and retreated to his hometown. The various division commanders of the 25th Army, such as You Guocai, Che Mingyi, Hou Zhidan, Song Xing, and Jiang Zaizhen, seeing that Mao did not compete with Wang, also expressed their obedience and supported Wang Jialie in order to preserve their positions and strength. However, although Mao retired to his hometown, he was not actually willing to give up the titles of army commander and chairman to Wang. Secretly, he was still carrying out a plan to regain his position and was secretly contacting various parties. He obtained the consent of You Guocai, Che Mingyi, Hou Zhidan, Jiang Zaizhen, and Song Xing. Mao also sent Li Shihai, the former director of his office in Chongqing, to Chongqing in secret to contact Liu Xiang of the 21st Army to ask for Liu's assistance in the future restoration of his position. Liu also readily agreed and encouraged him to launch the operation because Wang Jialie of Guizhou Province had a close friendship with Liu Wenhui of the 24th Army. If he did not help Mao attack Wang, and the 21st Army attacked the 24th Army, Wang Jialie would inevitably send troops to help Wenhui. Therefore, he used Mao Guangxiang to restrain Wang Jialie in order to weaken Wenhui's strength. At the same time, Hou Zhidan of the Mao faction of the Guizhou army also helped the 21st Army attack the 24th Army. This time, Liu Xiang captured Luxian, and Hou Zhidan of the Guizhou army played a powerful role. After Mao Guangxiang obtained Liu Xiang's support and the support of various generals, he took advantage of the completion of the Zhou Former Chairman's Memorial Hall to convene a meeting of representatives from various counties in Tong (under the pretext of participating in the completion ceremony of the memorial hall). The representatives of the counties also expressed their support. Seeing that the time was ripe, Mao then instructed Jiang Zaizhen of the Third Division stationed in Zunyi and You Guocai and Che Mingyi of Qianxi to deploy military affairs and prepare to

Page 12

launch an operation. After receiving the order, You Guocai and others issued a telegram in the name of various generals, requesting Mao to resume his position and advocating that Wang should be urged to step down and hand over the military and civilian administration through political means first. Otherwise, they would launch an attack. Jiang also intercepted various tax revenues in Zunyi for military use and divided his troops to occupy the area along the Wujiang River, with a great momentum to wave his troops into the province. Wang Jialie believed that the environment was dangerous and that his own strength was limited. If You Guocai, Che Mingyi, Hou Zhidan, and Song Xing unanimously united against him, it would be difficult to deal with. He immediately sent a telegram to Liu Wenhui, requesting assistance. However, Liu Wenhui had already lost the counties in northern Sichuan, southern Sichuan, and the eastern part, and Deng and Tian launched an attack in Chengdu, so he felt that it was difficult to cope with himself. He was naturally unable to intervene in the Guizhou affair. Wang was forced to send troops to attack Jiang Zaizhen first. In recent days, the Wujiang River has been shrouded in war clouds, but Jiang Zaizhen's strength is only five regiments. Therefore, he widely recruited bandits from central Guizhou and various places in Sichuan province to form an army to increase his strength. Mao Guangxiang also appointed Yang Qichang, the former Guizhou army division commander, as the independent division commander, and Shuang Qing as the independent brigade commander, to recruit bandits from the border area between Sichuan and Guizhou to form an army and go to the Wujiang River to fight. Mao Guangxiang himself has moved from Tong to Zunyi to command everything, while Hou Zhidan, who is against Wang and supports Mao, has now been reassigned to the 21st Army as the Sichuan-Guizhou Border Defense Commander, and he has stated that he will not intervene in the Guizhou war. As for You Guocai, Che Mingyi, Song Xing, and Jiang Zaizhen, they have already made it clear that they support Mao in reforming the Guizhou situation. Yesterday (November 25th), a telegram was received here stating that fierce fighting had broken out in the Zunyi area, with more than 500 casualties on both sides. You, Che, and others have also actually joined the fighting. You, Hou, and Che each led four regiments of troops and stationed themselves in Qingzhen and Guili, 60 miles away from Guiyang, taking a threatening stance towards Wang Jialie. The scope of the war is bound to expand. It is reported that Wang Jialie has now decided that if the war is unfavorable, he will retreat to Jiading and cooperate with the 24th Army to seek another opportunity to rise. (November 26th)

Opening of a Commercial District in Guangzhou's Dashatou 74

▲ Land Demarcation and Auction in Phases ▲ Relocation of Opium Dens, Gambling Houses, and Brothels First Guangzhou Correspondence: Dashatou in Guangzhou, originally an island near the Dongdi Guangzhou-Kowloon Railway Station, was initially inhabited by boat-dwelling Tanka people who built shacks and gathered there. Later, military authorities, considering its isolation from the city, established facilities there. Subsequently, aviation authorities also set up facilities in Dashatou, opening an airfield. Most of the Tanka residents relocated, and after several major fires, there are almost no Tanka shacks left. Recently, the air force moved to Shou Gou Ling, and new airfields and hangars were also established in the Shou Gou Ling military camp. Dashatou, a small island, no longer has the strict security of the past. The authorities, seeing its large area, decided to transform it into a commercial district and auction off the entire island's land. The Construction Department, Finance Department, and Municipal Government jointly planned this, and yesterday decided on the land prices and auction methods for Dashatou. The auction will be conducted in three phases, with each phase lasting six months. The first phase starts immediately, while the second and third phases will be implemented later. As for the land prices, they are divided into three grades: first-grade land is priced at 500 yuan per hua bing (a unit of area), second-grade land at 450 yuan per hua bing, and third-grade land at 400 yuan per hua bing. In the first phase, land facing east is classified as Grade A, land facing north and south as Grade B, and land facing west as Grade C. The land price for arcaded areas along roads will be charged at 50% of the auction price per bing. As for the existing Japanese-owned businesses, separate prices will be determined for their acquisition. When acquiring private properties, a notice will be published in the newspaper, and owners must register immediately, with a one-month deadline from the date of registration. The method of compensation for land prices will be determined separately. The transformation of Dashatou into a commercial district aims to develop a prosperous area as a preliminary step. However, to achieve prosperity, the first priority is to equip the area with entertainment venues. The authorities plan to order all opium dens, gambling houses, brothels, and pleasure boats in Guangzhou to relocate to Dashatou. However, it is difficult to force these establishments to relocate immediately, so a method of "banning through taxation" is being considered. It is stipulated that these establishments must relocate within six months. After six months, those who do not comply with the relocation order will have their original house rent doubled, starting from the seventh month. The landlords will collect this amount from their tenants and hand it over as an entertainment tax, which will be used to repair entertainment venues. After one year, those who still do not comply with the relocation order will have their original house rent tripled, starting from the thirteenth month. After one and a half years, those who still do not relocate will have their original house rent quadrupled, starting from the nineteenth month. In general, each phase lasts six months, with the tax increasing by one fold in each period. This escalating taxation will force them to be unable to maintain their businesses and voluntarily relocate. (November 24th)

Bean Cake Tax Dispute in Chao-Shan 75

▲ Customs detains imported bean cakes Shantou correspondence: Bean cake is the best fertilizer produced domestically, originating from Dalian, Andong, Niuzhuang, Hankou, and other places. Approximately 800,000 dan (a unit of weight) are shipped to Chao-Shan annually. The Taili Company in Shantou is contracted to collect a special tax on imported sulfuric acid fertilizers. This special tax is an additional charge for the construction of Zhongshan University's campus. The company remits 270,000 yuan to the Department of Finance annually, having been approved to handle this tax. However, the company, concealing the truth from its superiors, claimed that domestically produced bean cakes were also imported goods and should be taxed together. The superiors, believing this, immediately approved the collection. The company then notified various grain stores to inspect and tax the bean cakes in their warehouses, setting a deadline of November 24th for reporting and payment, with a tax of 8 jiao (a unit of currency) and 2.5 fen (a subunit of currency) per dan. Bean cake merchants were dissatisfied, arguing that bean cake is clearly made from domestic soybeans and peanuts, transported from the northern coast, so how could it be considered imported goods? Furthermore, the government's tax on imported sulfuric acid fertilizer was intended to preserve the sales of domestic bean cake. The Taili Company started operations on August 1st, and its announcement at the time mentioned this. Just over a hundred days have passed, and it cannot be so forgetful. The Shantou North-South Port Freight Association therefore decided to telegraph the provincial government to object, and simultaneously petitioned the Eastern District Pacification Commissioner's Office, the Shantou Municipal Government, and the Public Security Bureau to order the police to protect the goods and prevent the company from detaining merchant goods, awaiting a government resolution. Meanwhile, Chen Shaowen and others were dispatched to the province to petition the Department of Finance to stop the collection of bean cake tax, and to explain that if bean cake cannot be shipped to Shantou for sale this winter, farmland will lack fertilizer next spring, making it difficult to expect a good harvest, which would have a significant impact. However, the provincial government's attitude is still unknown. Furthermore, yesterday a batch of bean cake shipped from Yingkou arrived, and the Taili Company immediately sent inspectors to force various firms to report and pay fees to the company. Mingfeng and other firms, because the ship was chartered and could not delay its departure, had no choice but to report and pay tax to the company. It is said that according to the company's tax collection method, the Shantou bean cake tax alone could generate over one million yuan annually. The Taili Company's contracted tax on fertilizers for the entire province is only 270,000 yuan, so its profits are unexpectedly high, while the government and the people both suffer losses. Therefore, it is not acceptable to bean cake merchants.

Plea from All Circles in Beiping: Do Not Relocate Ancient Artifacts 76

Seeing reports that the Central Government was planning to move the ancient artifacts of the Forbidden City to Luoyang for preservation, all circles in Beiping jointly sent a telegram, stating the advantages and disadvantages, and requesting that the proposal be reconsidered. The telegram is transcribed below: ▲ Telegram One: We have just read reports stating that the Central Political Council has decided to transport the ancient artifacts of the Beiping Forbidden City to Luoyang. All the people and organizations in the city are extremely alarmed, believing that the Central Government is abandoning Beiping and cutting off the people's lives. The cultural development plan for the prosperity of Beiping is paramount. Without the ancient artifacts of the Forbidden City, culture would have no basis, and foreign tourists and researchers would have no direction. Beiping would inevitably decline day by day, making it difficult to survive. The intention to transport the artifacts to Luoyang is solely to avoid the enemy. However, it must be understood that the way to establish a nation is to resist the enemy, not to avoid them. Retreating step by step is the way to national ruin. Unnecessarily showing weakness to others is to abandon Beiping. Does Beiping have land and people that will also be moved? If not, why are ancient artifacts considered more important, and the people and land less important? Even for the sake of the ancient artifacts, moving them to Luoyang does not guarantee their safety. Beiping is the location of embassies from various countries, and the Forbidden City is close at hand, under the watchful eyes of all. Ancient artifacts are related to culture, not the same as war materials. Even if the enemy is strong and violent, they should not dare to destroy them wantonly. Moreover, the League of Nations is seeking a resolution to the dispute between the two countries. The responsibility for the past lies with the other side, and they are trying to shirk it. If they were to add troops to Beiping without reason, the responsibility would be even greater. Anyone with vision would not dare to do this at this time. Therefore, it is unwise to create panic. Luoyang is not a safe place. Those who know the past should know that there are many bandits there. Transporting ancient artifacts there is like sending a sheep into a tiger's den. The Forbidden City in Beiping has deep moats and high walls, making defense easy. Supervision from all sides is also strict. Luoyang has nothing, so how can it be preserved? We fear that it will not be destroyed by the enemy, but various disasters will be enough to endanger the ancient artifacts. This is a complete reversal of reality and ideals. There are many rumors outside that moving the artifacts to Luoyang is only a pretext. Once they leave Beiping, they will be transferred and sold. This is contrary to reason, so it is no wonder people are suspicious. In summary, the ancient artifacts of the Forbidden City and the people of Beiping share a common destiny. If we seek safety on the spot, the people will do their best to help. If the Central Government does not love Beiping, does not listen to the people's opinions, acts selfishly for the benefit of a few, and disregards the consequences, the people of Beiping will lie down on the tracks and perish with the ancient artifacts. We urge the leaders of the Party and the nation to consider this carefully. If the reports are true, please cancel the decision immediately. If there is no such plan, please make a clear statement to dispel public doubts. In the future, the method of preservation should be made public to avoid manipulation, so that the ancient artifacts can be preserved permanently. This is the fervent hope of all organizations. We respectfully submit this telegram and humbly request your consideration. Beiping Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Public Offices of Autonomous Districts in Beiping, Beiping General Labor Union, Beiping Farmers' Association, Youth Association, Education Association, Good Youth Association ▲ Telegram Two: Reports state that the Central Political Council held a meeting the other day and resolved to move the ancient artifacts of the Beiping Forbidden City to Luoyang for safekeeping, ordering the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Railways to be responsible for transportation. The merchants and people here are perplexed, believing that the essence of culture has been gathered here for hundreds of years, attracting the attention of the world. Once it is moved, it will lose its center of gravity. This is the first point. These precious objects have been cherished for many years, and we are still worried about damage. The railway transportation is precarious in every way. This is the second point. The walls and palaces here are not afraid of petty theft. Furthermore, we are building secret vaults, making them even more secure. Luoyang has broken walls and ruins, with wind and rain howling. In terms of safekeeping, which is better? This is the third point. The national capital has already been determined, and moving the ancient artifacts to Luoyang will encourage people to despise it. This is the fourth point. If there is a compelling reason, we ask, if we can go, can't the enemy? It only shows weakness to others and increases the enemy's intentions. This is the fifth point. If the government takes this action, it indicates abandonment of Beiping. How can we encourage the morale of those who are determined to resist the enemy to the death? How can we consolidate the hearts of the people to resist the enemy united? This association, representing hundreds of thousands of merchants and people in the city, vows to express solidarity with various popular organizations to prevent its implementation and to coexist with the ancient artifacts. We implore you to immediately reconsider this proposal to avoid misunderstandings at home and abroad. It is a blessing for the national essence, a blessing for the country! Beiping Municipal Chamber of Commerce

Opening of the Zhejiang Agricultural Products Exhibition 77

▲ Six to Seven Thousand Exhibits The Zhejiang Provincial Agricultural Products Exhibition, which has been in preparation by the Construction Department for two months, is now ready. The opening ceremony is scheduled for 9:00 AM today (December 1st), and the exhibition will open to the public from 2:00 PM. The exhibition venue has been set up in recent days. The response to the call for agricultural products has been exceptionally enthusiastic. As of the afternoon of the 30th, submissions had been received from 62 counties. Other affiliated institutions of the Construction Department, such as rice, wheat, cotton, silk, forestry, and entomology, as well as agricultural, sericultural, and aquatic product schools, have also submitted special products. The Huangyan tangerines, Yueqing pears, Hangzhou persimmons, Xiangshan and Taishun medicinal herbs, Xinchang and Songyang tobacco leaves, and Linhai, Haiyan, and Yuhuan aquatic products are particularly famous. The rice seeds submitted by various counties are numerous, reaching six to seven hundred varieties. There are also many imported varieties. A total of over three thousand items have been sent by various counties. Affiliated institutions of the Construction Department have also sent over three thousand items. The exhibition is divided into two major sections. Products from various counties are classified and displayed for competition and observation. Products from affiliated institutions of the Construction Department and vocational schools are classified by institution as a reference. Therefore, the products from various counties will be thoroughly reviewed after the closing ceremony, and ranks will be determined to award certificates. Zeng Yangfu, Director of the Construction Department, believes that the agricultural products exhibition contains the nature of improving agricultural products and promoting high-quality seeds, so the mission is significant. Therefore, he rushed back to the provincial capital from eastern Zhejiang on the afternoon of the 30th to personally preside over the opening ceremony today. It is reported that after the opening ceremony today, the association will invite agricultural experts Xu Shuji, Wang Jinwu, Zhang Fancun, and Chen Shimin to broadcast lectures on agricultural issues from 2:00 PM to 3:00 PM every day. It has also been agreed with the Central Aviation School to use airplanes to distribute various promotional materials on the 1st, 4th, and 7th of this month.

Nanhui 78

▲ Frequent Bandit Alarms During Winter Defense The county is currently carrying out winter defense measures, but theft cases still occur from time to time. Last night at 10:00 PM, at the residence of Feng Jinru and Feng Yinru in Fengjiazhai, about three li (a unit of distance) outside the North Gate, six bandits suddenly arrived with pistols and sharp blades. They broke into the house and tied up Feng Jinru and others with ropes. Feng Yinru's wife resisted and was violently stabbed in the right leg by the bandits, sustaining two injuries and bleeding profusely. The bandits then began searching, looting gold and silver jewelry, clothing, and other items worth over 300 yuan. The First Branch of the Public Security Bureau outside the East Gate rushed to pursue them after hearing the alarm, but the bandits had already gone far. Furthermore, at the home of Zhao Xingyan, a farmer in Nianwu Tu near Hangtou Zhen, over ten bandits suddenly arrived at approximately the same time the night before, wielding iron rods, breaking into the house through the windows. They immediately tied up and beat Zhao Xingyan and others, forcing him to reveal the location of hidden silver. Zhao Xingyan firmly refused to speak and was burned with candles and struck with iron rods, causing burns to his head and serious injuries. The bandits searched for a long time, looting silver, clothing, and other items, and then left in a swagger.

At that time, the Ministry of Finance approved the request, stipulating that after the expiration of the period, the Suzhou Provincial Government should not request an extension under any name. Wuxi 80

▲ Rampant Corruption in Tax Collection Agency With the approval of the Provincial Government, Shu Shifu of the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance issued a notice to all counties to uniformly establish tax collection agencies. All sales and transfers of houses and land would be officially collected and processed by the tax collection agency, and official stamped receipts would be issued at any time. Wang Li, Director of the Local Finance Bureau, followed the order and organized the agency, appointing Lu Dingxin as the director and selecting sixteen staff members from the district offices. The tax collection fee was 4 jiao 5 fen per 100 yuan, and it was also announced that various fees such as book-giving rice should be abolished. However, the district offices, upon hearing this, were greatly dissatisfied because their income had decreased sharply. Therefore, they went around lobbying the authorities, tacitly agreeing to collect the book-giving rice and other illegal fees in secret in addition to the tax collection fee. Rampant corruption caused a heavier burden for ordinary villagers, who dared to be angry but dared not speak out. Therefore, although the tax collection agency was established, it was actually just a change of name, and the system was no different from the district office system. ▲ Two Cases of Robbery and Assault The family of Widow Guo Dongshi in Qianjia village, Nanfangquan, District 14, was poor. She had a son and a daughter-in-law who helped with farming. Suddenly, at approximately 10:00 PM the night before, two bandits speaking with a strong northern accent and wearing blue cloths on their faces broke into the house. They shone flashlights around the room where Ms. Guo was sleeping. Ms. Guo woke up from her dream. One of the bandits immediately stabbed her with an iron sword. Ms. Guo used her hand to grab the iron sword and held it tightly. The bandits struggled to snatch it away, pushing Ms. Guo to the ground and scratching her throat with their fingers. In a moment of desperation, Ms. Guo immediately shouted, "Catch the robbers!" Seeing the situation was unfavorable, the bandits abandoned the sword and fled empty-handed. After inspection, there were no losses. She immediately reported this to Lu Difan, the head of District 14, who then reported it to the county government for investigation. Also, at approximately 2:00 AM the night before, the house of Zheng Quangen in Nanjie, Yuqi Town, District 15, was suddenly attacked by five or six bandits armed with sharp blades, who threatened them to remain silent and looted at will. They also used the sharp blades to stab three wounds in Zheng's head. After inspection, the losses were estimated at over 20 yuan. The victim reported this to the 15th Public Security Branch, requesting the arrest of the bandits.

Changshu 81

▲ Former Head of the Second District Accused of Embezzlement Hu Sheng, the former head of the Second District, has been repeatedly sued by Yang Hongyuan and other citizens of the district for allegedly embezzling public funds during his tenure. The lawsuit mainly stated that when the Songhu War broke out this spring, the army arrived in the county to defend it. He had constructed defense projects and installed military telephones, etc. The materials used in Meili and other areas were all purchased by District Head Hu. However, Hu falsely reported the quantities and embezzled huge amounts of money. Just take the telephone lead wire as an example. According to the installation certificate, 350 jin (a unit of weight) were actually used, while his reimbursement request was for 557 jin. After receiving the report, the county government repeatedly held court hearings, but District Head Hu did not appear in court. Later, County Magistrate Tan, in order to ease public anger, transferred the two district heads because Pan Zhengfen, the head of the Twelfth District, was also accused of embezzlement, so as to achieve the best of both worlds. However, the plaintiff, Yang Hongyuan, still refused to give up and filed a lawsuit with the Wu County District Court. He was summoned in mid-month, but Hu did not appear, so a warrant was issued. He was summoned on the 28th of this month. On that day, the plaintiff, the defendant, and the witness, Lu Shaozeng, all complied with the summons and went to Suzhou to await the hearing. The District Court was opened for investigation by Prosecutor Lu Wenqin. The plaintiff and the witness stated the above, while the defendant Hu and the accountant Tao Yu both denied the previous facts and attached receipts from the Third Battalion of the First Brigade of the Forty-seventh Division. As a result, the court ordered the defendant Hu Sheng and Tao Yu to be released on bail. Now, people in Meili Township, because the transferred District Head Pan Zhengfen had previously been accused of embezzlement by the original township chiefs and had not made public any financial matters since March, have requested the county government to remove him by Lu Shaozeng and other members of the Party in a petition signed by 120 people. ▲ An Elderly Man from Suzhou Comes to Changshu to Commit Suicide Huang Yongkang, an elderly man from Suzhou, suddenly left Suzhou for Changshu on the 24th for unknown reasons. His family searched everywhere for him, but there was no trace of him. Just as they were worrying, they suddenly received a letter on the 25th, stating that he was tired of life and would not return home. His family matters could be properly handled, etc. After reading it, his son was terrified. He checked the postmark, which was from Changshu, so he immediately took a boat to Changshu to find him. It was not until the night of the 28th that he was found in the Fuchang Inn in Beizhao Lane here. Meeting his family, he was overjoyed and frightened. The next morning, they returned to Suzhou together.

The cases in the countryside were all impersonated by others. ▲ Jiangsu Plans to Establish a Provincial Water Police Bureau Recently, due to the lack of security and the rise of bandits, navigation has become especially dangerous. News of river steamers being robbed has been heard from time to time. Although there is a provincial public security team on the water, the jurisdiction is vast and each district is self-governing. It is difficult to achieve a consistent and coordinated bandit suppression effort. It is reported that in order to ensure the safety of water travelers and unify the command of the provincial water public security teams, the province plans to establish a provincial water police bureau to command the provincial public security teams in various districts. Its authority will be the same as the former water police department, and the organization will be entirely modeled after the current Zhejiang water police bureau. It is currently in the planning stage, and its implementation should not be far off. It is said that the counties will also expand their water public security forces to supplement the shortage of police force in the township public security bureaus. After implementation, the existing Su-Song Water Bandit Suppression Command will also be abolished to unify power. ▲ Construction Department Inspects the Zhenjiang Reservoir Project According to the report submitted by the Zhenjiang County Government, the Zhenjiang County Reservoir Engineering Committee has gradually completed the new and old mountain reservoirs in Shangdang, Suifeng, Gaozi, and other townships in this session. ▲ Seven Japanese Plainclothes Detectives Illegally Arrested ▲ Two Were Detained by the Annamite Police, While the Rest Fled A Korean man surnamed Jin, around 50 years old, originally lived on the second floor of No. 2 Ruyi Lane, Lan Wei Ai Road, French Concession. This Year's Trend in Foreign Rice Imports 89

▲ Index from January to September

▲ April as the Peak, the issue of regulating rice prices is currently attracting much attention from various sectors. This is because our country is originally an agricultural nation, with farmers accounting for about three-quarters of the national population. Therefore, agricultural products are of great importance to our country's economy and the people's livelihood, especially rice, which people need daily for their lives. The reason for the drop in grain prices this year is due to the bumper harvest of domestic produce, the competition from foreign rice, and the obstacles in transportation and shipping, which have led to difficulties in sales and caused this serious problem. Although there is no precise investigation into the bumper harvest situation, it is generally understood that ordinary yields have increased by several percent, while excellent yields have even doubled. Regarding the competitive sales of foreign rice, according to the "International Trade Statistics" compiled and printed by the International Trade Bureau, the import index of foreign rice from February to September of this year (with the average of 1926 as the base number) is: (February) 89.18, (March) 151.94, (April) 176.10, (May) 168.48, (June) 115.28, (July) 111.21, (August) 98.62, (September) 75.04. The above numbers show a gradual decreasing trend with April as the peak. Furthermore, most of these imports are destined for Guangdong, as the transportation of rice from Jiangnan and Jiangbei is inconvenient, making the import of rice from Vietnam and Burma more convenient and cheaper. Therefore, the entire problem lies in the obstacles and inconvenience of domestic transportation. According to He Bingxian, Director of the International Trade Bureau, if one wants to find a solution to the rice price issue, the Ministry of Industry, the Ministry of Interior, the Ministry of Communications, and the Ministry of Railways must work together. The International Trade Bureau, recognizing the severity of this issue, is discussing effective measures to adopt, even without any instructions.

Japanese Fishing Boats 91

Dumping Small Yellow Croaker

▲ Fish Markets are Actually Selling on Consignment

▲淮輪Industry is Complaining Greatly

According to the Central News Agency, the Japanese fishing boat "Eying Maru" again imported a large batch of fresh fish on the 28th, totaling 697 boxes, all of which were small yellow croaker. Starting from the 29th, Hengchang, Yongxing, Qianmao, Damao, Yongmao, and other fish markets in the 16th ward sold them on consignment at extremely low prices. According to people in the fishing industry, the domestic bucket-headed goods from Ningbo and other places were priced at around 16 yuan per担on the same day, while the fish brought in by the "Eying Maru" fishing boat were priced at only 10 to 12 yuan, greatly affecting domestic fishermen. The fishing boat industry is also secretly complaining, daring to be angry but not daring to speak out.

News Compilation of the Association for Aiding Northeastern Refugees 94

▲ Overseas Chinese Enthusiastically Donate ▲ Representatives from Beyond the Pass Report The following is a summary of important news from yesterday from the Shanghai United Association of Charitable Organizations for Aiding Northeastern Refugees: ▲ Kong Yongzhi's Letter. Kong Xiangxi, Special Envoy for Industrial Investigation of Various Countries, sent a letter from his New York office at 51st Street to Xu Shiying, Xiong Xiling, Wang Xiating, Qu Yingguang, Zhao Xien, Wang Jue, Wang Han and others, saying: Jingren, Bing San, Jiatang, Wenliu, Jinqing, Yiheng, Hanzhi, gentlemen: Across the vast ocean, all my thoughts are with you. During my trip to America, I passed through Honolulu, San Francisco, Chicago, New York, and other places, where I either received representatives from overseas Chinese or attended gatherings of overseas Chinese merchants and organizations. I explained the difficult situation in the Northeast and the details of the efforts of charitable organizations in Shanghai, and I informed them of the establishment of the Shanghai United Association, requesting that donations be sent to you for effective use. The overseas Chinese merchants were all deeply moved upon hearing this. I am confident that with your enthusiasm and promotion, donations will continue to increase. I have already sent donation booklets and publications to various ports to widely solicit donations. My industrial investigation in America will take another two or three weeks, and I plan to travel to Europe at the end of the month. I am writing to inform you of my situation and to pay my respects. Respectfully, Kong Xiangxi, November 5th. ▲ Using Entertainment Donations. The association had previously written to the government requesting that the entertainment donations collected be allocated to aid Northeastern refugees. This time, when Xu Jingren heard that Lan Ting, Li Zubao and others were passing through Beijing, they discussed it again. The association received a telegram from Xu, Lan, and Li yesterday, stating that Minister Zhu said that once the additional entertainment donations are implemented and have generated a significant amount, he will invite representatives from all sectors to discuss the distribution. The English representatives left Beijing for Shanghai yesterday afternoon. ▲ Aid Work in the Northeast. The association received a letter from Feng Shifen, a representative from beyond the pass, stating: The previous letter mentioned that the Bank of China remitted 50,000 Shanghai dollars, which has been received. This amount is equivalent to 59,450 Harbin dollars. If converted to cash, it would be about 49,600 Shanghai dollars, with Shanghai dollars being worth 7% more. The association mostly uses Harbin dollars. However, the exchange rate for Harbin dollars fluctuates daily. Currently, 10,000 sets of cotton clothes are being made here, requiring 34,500 Harbin dollars, plus approximately 500 dollars for shipping. The remainder has been remitted to Harbin to purchase aid supplies. Fenfeng left Changchun on the 24th to go to Harbin to work with Luo Shulao (named Zhenyu) and others in the Temporary Disaster Relief Association to jointly handle the distribution. The relief tickets will be under the sole name of this association and 20,000 have already been printed with a stamp, under the name of the Shanghai Nine Charitable Organizations Joint Relief Association Office in Harbin. ▲ Xiamen Remits Relief Funds. The association received 100 yuan from Xiamen University to aid Northeastern refugees. ▲ Qu Wenliu's Letter. He will then send a receipt for verification. Please inquire with the Chamber of Commerce and colleagues in Shanghai whether to start a disaster relief Dharma assembly in Shanghai to facilitate coordination.

▲ Saving Money from Candy and Snacks, One Yuan ▲ Purchasing Carnival Tickets to Aid Northeastern Refugees

Since the Northeastern Refugee Relief Carnival, jointly organized by the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the General Labor Union, the Accountants Association, and the Lawyers Association, was announced in major newspapers, enthusiastic patriots have been sending letters to purchase tickets. Yesterday, among the mail received by the association was a letter from a 13-year-old elementary school student and a 7-year-old kindergarten student who were willing to save the candy and snack money given to them daily by their father to donate one yuan to purchase a ticket. Although the wording was simple, their passionate patriotism overflowed from their words. The original letter is transcribed below: We all hate the Japanese. Teacher often talks about it, and Dad also talks about it. Last night, Dad read the newspaper advertisement to us and talked about it for a long time. I am willing to start today, after school, not to eat snacks. Mom gives me ten copper coins, save one a month to buy a ticket. My sister is also willing to save to buy a ticket to send. Take the money. Elementary School Student, Yang Shixun, 12 years old. My brother loves the country, and I love the country too. Yang Juefang, 7 years old. November 27th, No. 1, Jingxiu Lane, Wudong Road, Xiaoximen. ▲ Social Affairs Bureau Employees Donate Salaries. Li Liejun on National Salvation 97

▲ Talking to Central News Agency Reporters

According to the Central News Agency, the Fourth Plenary Session of the Third Central Committee has been set for the 15th of this month in Nanjing. At this time of internal and external troubles, the Chinese people should be united from top to bottom to jointly discuss major plans for national salvation. The Central Committee members staying in Shanghai have decided to gather in the capital before the meeting to attend the conference and have drafted a general proposal to be submitted at the conference. However, in order to solicit the opinions of the Central Committee members in Guangdong on the Plenary Session, Liu Luyin, Bai Wenwei, Cheng Qian, Zhang Zhiben, and four others have gone to Guangdong for discussions. Regarding this news, Li Liejun, a Central Committee member staying in Shanghai, made the following statement to the Central News Agency reporters yesterday:

▲ Guangdong Committee Members Cannot Attend Fully. According to the statement, the Fourth Plenary Session of the Third Central Committee is extremely important for the survival of the nation, so the opinions of all parties should be consistent. Therefore, Liu Luyin, Bai Wenwei, Cheng Qian, and Zhang Zhiben are currently going south to meet with the Central Committee members staying in Guangdong to solicit opinions and inquire about the general proposal drafted by the Central Committee members staying in Shanghai, so as to gather a wide range of views. Furthermore, given the large number of Northeastern refugees entering the customs and the lack of relief measures, Bai and others will also consult with the Guangdong side on solutions for refugee relief, so that the displaced Northeastern compatriots will not starve to death. Whether all of the Central Committee members staying in Guangdong will be able to attend the Plenary Session is still undecided. It seems certain that Hu Hanmin will not be able to attend in Nanjing.

▲ The Reasons for Internal Strife Are No More Than Three. Liu also said that internal strife in our country has increased year by year. Examining the causes of internal strife, there are no more than three: (1) The government cannot get on the right track due to the inability to achieve equal governance and realize national politics, so that politics can be put on the right track; (2) Sun's doctrine cannot be fully realized. Sun's Three Principles of the People are the doctrine of national salvation. At this time of national crisis, the members of our party must take on the responsibility of saving the country and realizing the Three Principles of the People; (3) People's hearts have fallen into pessimism. To save China from danger, we must first save people's hearts from falling into pessimism. Lao Tzu said, "Sorrow is greater than the death of the heart." Although the hearts of the Chinese people are not completely dead, they have fallen into a state of pessimism. Pessimism is the first step towards the death of the heart. The way to save it is to wait for the Plenary Session to decide on a plan and gradually implement it step by step. Then the internal strife will stop, and the government will be put on the right track. Sun's doctrine will be fully implemented, and the pessimism of the people's hearts will naturally disappear. The hope will arise spontaneously, hope will become a reality, and reality will become a belief. Then pessimism will disappear and optimism will come, and the country will have a future. If the situation after the Plenary Session remains the same as it is now, then the country's future is truly worrying.
