Grains 183

Rice Market Situation Stable 184

(Shanghai South) The sources of various groups are five or more than ten. Due to the end of the year for Guoli (National Calendar), the firms on both sides are preparing to end and collect accounts, so the transaction is quiet. The Su Tong group called for a rise of a few jiao. Early and late rice arrival and sales are even. The market is not rising or falling. Foreign Du sharp top rice is somewhat weaker (Xin Zha) Ships from the Yejidun area have not arrived, and the number is not much, about fifteen or sixteen. The sales market in this street is slightly thick. No honor or disgrace. Thin rice and early rice are sold as they arrive, and the shape is hard five fen. The price of rice from the river is 3,000 shi (a unit of volume).

Ke Xian Rice Arrival and Sales are Both Strong 185

丨The Fujian group has a strong appetite丨 Yesterday, the Ke Xian rice situation was active, and the market atmosphere was good. Because there were not many arrivals in recent days, after arriving, they were sold as they arrived, and there was no accumulation in the market. The production price was fair, and the handling was also quite appropriate. The Fujian province groups have very strong appetites, and they especially need Hunan Ke Xian rice, so the market price is firm, which is very different from the sluggishness of foreign rice. Yesterday, more than 600 bags of Hunan machine oil rice were opened at a price of 8 yuan and 8 or 9 jiao, and 110 bags of rice were opened at a price of 7 yuan and 3 jiao and a half. Also, 200 bags of machine red rice were opened at a price of 8 yuan, and 200 bags of rough red rice were opened at a price of 6 yuan and 8 jiao and a half. Wuhu Yuan rice, 73 bags, was opened at a price of 10 yuan. Except for a small number of purchases by the Beiyang group, they were all purchased by the Fujian group.

November Futures Flour Delivery Completed 186

▲Old Car Brand 2,000 Bags▲

Yesterday, the end of the month delivery futures market lacked volume and the spot market was also sluggish. The monthly futures delivery has also been completed. According to statistics, only Fufeng Factory delivered 2,000 bags of red and blue car flour, which were received by No. 3. There were no other deliveries. These 2,000 bags from Fufeng were also due to a mistake in crushing, and the total number had to be delivered. This is because the factories do not have much stock, and the cost is too high, so they do not bother to deliver spot goods.

A Total of Seven Carloads Were Delivered 187

Last month, only seven carloads were delivered to the exchange, which were delivered by Yuanyu and others, and received by Huafeng Factory. There were few spot wheat arrivals and stocks in the market, so there were very few chips. Even the number of direct deliveries was not many. Approximately 30 carloads were delivered in advance before the middle of the month.

Chicago Wheat Prices Mixed 188

Sin Fung Trading Company reports that on Tuesday (the 29th), Chicago wheat fell initially due to long liquidation but rebounded due to poor winter production reports. As a result, prices were mixed. On the 28th, the total trading volume was 30 million bushels. The market prices for the 29th are listed below:

Closing prices compared to the previous day: December futures 41.875, down 0.20; May futures 46.750, down 0.125; July futures 47.500, down 1.250.

Silk and Tea White Factory Business to Europe is Quiet 189

Yesterday, the Shanghai foreign silk market presented a sluggish appearance. Although overseas silk prices have risen, the exchange rate is still rigid, rising in name but weakening in reality. Chinese silk merchants believe that it is difficult to sell at a loss, and the market atmosphere is quiet. Yesterday, only Xinfu entered the Linwei brand's top No. 2, Qilibai, dried silk, 30 packages, at a price of 520 taels.

Luzhuang Zhenmei French Sales Active 190

Yesterday, in the Shanghai foreign tea market, British merchants such as Shangjinlong and Xiehe received telegrams from Morocco requesting Zhenmei green tea from Wuyuan and Tunxi, etc., and began to handle it. The entire city talked about 600 boxes, and the market price did not fluctuate. Needle eyebrow pearl tea and other items also had some scattered transactions, and the prices were firm. However, the Russian Assistance Association's recognition price for the Gongxi item has been particularly harsh recently, and the market price of goods from Wuyuan Northwest and other regions has fallen to 27 or 28 taels, the lowest level since the outbreak of the European War. Chinese tea merchants have suffered huge losses.

Metal Small Finish Nails Rising Unceasingly 191

Yesterday, the metal market situation remained the same as the previous day. Although the Jiangxi group suddenly rose in customer sales, the Sichuan group stopped operating due to the low water level in the upper reaches of the Yangtze River. The appetite of other groups, such as Tianjin, Qingdao, and Hankou, was similar to before. The factories' business did not improve significantly yesterday. According to investigations, the total daily transactions of various goods reached more than 4,000. Among the colors, small finish nails have been soaring in price due to the extremely small amount of goods in the market. Three-fen nails are estimated at 14 taels, four-fen nails at 13 taels, five-fen nails at 12 taels and 5 qian, and six-fen nails at 13 taels, which is 5 qian to 1 tael higher than before. However, the underlying inventory is extremely depleted, resulting in buyers having no goods to buy. According to news from industry sources, this batch of goods will arrive next month, so there is no need to worry about shortages in the market. Other goods, such as plain white iron, corrugated iron, British copper plates, angle iron, new lead wire, and shear iron, were all traded in the market yesterday, but there was no change in market prices.

Free Talk

Short Story

The Pearl of Toledo 206

— By P. Merimee, translated by Bingzhi

Who can tell me which is more beautiful, the sun when it rises or when it sets? Who can tell me which is the most beautiful tree, the olive or the almond? Who can tell me which are the bravest people, the Valencians or the Andalusians? Who can tell me which is the most beautiful woman's face? I tell you who is the most beautiful woman: it is Arode Vargas, the Pearl of Toledo.

The black man Duzani ordered his spear to be brought, his shield to be brought; his spear he held in his right hand, his shield hung around his neck. He went down to his stable, where he gazed upon his forty-four mares one by one. He said, "Bercha is the strongest; I will bring back the Pearl of Toledo on her broad back, or else I will never return to Cordoba." He set out, riding his horse, and reached Toledo, where he met an old man near Zaggadan. "Good old man, please deliver this letter to Mr. Judea, Mr. Judea de Sarzana. If he is a man, he will come to the Alma Maimon spring to fight me. The Pearl of Toledo shall belong to one of us." The old man took the letter and gave it to Count de Sarzana, who was playing chess with the Pearl of Toledo. The Count read the letter, the letter of challenge, and slammed his hand on the table, knocking everything off. He immediately stood up and ordered his spear to be brought, his good horse to be brought; and the Pearl of Toledo also stood up, trembling all over, for she knew he was going to duel. "Lord Judea, Mr. Judea de Sarzana, please stay, I beg you, please stay here and play chess with me." "I will play no more chess, I am going to play with spears near the Alma Maimon spring." Arode's tears could not stop him, for nothing can stop a knight from dueling. So the Pearl of Toledo put on her cloak, mounted her mule, and went to the Alma Maimon spring. The grass around the spring was red. The water was also red. But what dyed the grass red, dyed the spring red, was not the blood of a Christian. The black man Duzani lay sleeping, facing the sky; Mr. Judea's spear was broken in his chest; the remaining blood was gradually disappearing. His mare Bercha looked at him with tears, for she could not heal her master's spear wound. The Pearl of Toledo dismounted from her mule. "Knight, be brave! You will live, and you can marry a beautiful Moless girl in the future; my hands know how to heal the spear wounds left by my warriors." "Ah, such a pure pearl, such a beautiful pearl, please pull out the shard of the spear that cut open my chest! This cold spear makes me freeze and shiver." She approached without suspicion; but he mustered his strength and slashed that beautiful face with the blade of his waist knife.

Address Before the Curtain 207

[Free Talk] can be regarded as a free [stage]. On this [stage], we can freely [perform], that is, freely [talk]. Until yesterday, the [performance] on this stage came to an end and the curtain closed. From today onwards, new activities begin and the curtain will open again. We won't talk too much about what's inside, just watch. However, before the audience is eager to know what's behind the curtain, we [people on stage] must briefly state our attitude.

We believe that everything in the world is progressing and becoming modern. Firstly, it should be theoretically and secondly, it is practically necessary. We believe that our life's cultivation greatly depends on literature and art, and it is a natural fact that literature and art should progress and modernize, and need to progress and modernize. Although we cannot report everything in advance about what we [perform on this stage] in the future in terms of programs, we must firmly establish our foothold for progress and modernity, even if it is some clowning or some posturing, we dare not deal with it casually.

But we have to bring the conversation back a little. Although we are not willing to perform monkey shows, imitating human behavior, to win the audience's smile, we are not willing to sing a few "eighteen touches, lovesickness in the fifth watch," or hum a few lines of "[clouds are light, wind is gentle, near noon]," to cater to the general shallow tastes, but we never want to sing a high tune, raise any banners, blow any horns, or send out any dignified [seemingly serious] mighty army, to promote any doctrine, and force the tastes of individuals or a small group of people on the majority. We only believe that the elements of life, literature and art, should and need to progress and modernize; at the same time, we don't want to be too far from the audience, [playing gongs and drums and singing operas ourselves], only [cheering in the background]. The curtain is opening, the free [stage] is appearing, and the people on stage are freely [performing], just watch. 乂乂乂乂

[The Weather is Fine Today!] 208

— Ye Shengtao

[Free Talk], this is a phantom-like noun. In the time of Qin Shihuang, if two people met on the road, stopped and talked a sentence or two, they would commit a capital crime, and what they talked about was not asked. Later, although there were no such straightforward and simple laws, on the one hand, there were model-making creeds, teaching people how to talk; on the other hand, there were so many laws, prohibiting people from talking about what they were not allowed to talk about. Under this dual pressure, is there still [Free Talk]?

Some of the discussions we hear and some of the texts we see are all surviving in the narrow gaps of this dual pressure. Only by not touching this side or offending that side can they be said and written, and we can hear and see them. If this limit is exceeded, the discussions can only be swallowed into the stomach and let them rot; as for the texts, they are split into editions, destroyed, and prohibited from delivery. Their disasters are more than one. So we have no chance to hear and see them.

The environment is like this, and people become unusually alert and smooth. How to be able to turn freely in the narrow gaps of dual pressure has become a compulsory course for people who establish words and hold opinions. If one studies this subject too well, one may even have an illusion, shrinking the narrow gap in which one is located even narrower. Let me give an example. Recently, many scholars in Beiping advocated designating Beiping as a cultural city, withdrawing military equipment, and avoiding the ravages of Japanese airplanes and cannons; but in their written opinions, they only vaguely referred to [the enemy], and the word [Japan] was never seen. They probably thought this way: if they explained it clearly in this written opinion of [planning ahead], saying it was for Japan's sake, it would be too embarrassing for Japan.

Wanting to talk about Mr. Zhang, fearing that Mr. Zhang would be suspicious, not talking. Wanting to talk about Mr. Li, fearing that Mr. Li would be angry, not talking. Let's talk about A and B, but fearing that Mr. Zhao and Mr. Wang, who are related to A and B, would be unhappy, so it's better not to talk. So talk about the weather. But saying the weather is bad may offend this silent and speechless nature, and suddenly a gust of strong wind and rain will come, hurting the head and wetting the clothes; this is still not acceptable. [Pushing a cart against a wall], only saying the weather is good is the only appropriate way. So, when two people meet, they often say in unison, [The weather is fine today!]

Written After the Feast, Amidst the Scattered Dishes 209

— Zi

丨Recording a certain banquet丨

A group of [heroes] who wield pens gathered at a restaurant in a corner of Fourth Avenue. The [heroes] totaled twenty-four 丨丨twenty men and four women. Among them were two pairs of [wives-to-be], one pair being Mr. Li Dachao and Mrs. Wang Xiaoying, and the other pair being the [highly respected] veteran Mr. Chen Wangdao and his editor-in-chief Weiyin's wife, Ms. Cai Cai.

It's hard to say they were all [heroes], but perhaps because they had never fought before, they were not very familiar with each other. So, in a group of [occasional whispers], someone hurried to call Bingxin, who was [enlisting in the army], as Ding Ling, who was [in the dark], and someone hurried to call Ms. Cai, who was editing Weiyin, as Lu Yin, and some people were quietly asking [which one is humorous] Lin Yutang? Which one is the stunning Zhang Ziping?

After a flurry of activity, the heroes each occupied a seat. Then, slowly, the floor was littered with melon seed shells, the air was filled with cigarette rings, and a faint smile hung on the face of each [hero], waiting for another [hero]'s question, looking for a suitable topic of conversation. Amidst a group of scattered voices, every happy heart was active.

After taking their seats, the heroes were divided into three piles in a line. During the banquet, Miss Bingxin eagerly asked about Mr. Zhang Ziping's newly built house, new creations, and when he would invite everyone to dinner, while Mr. Zhang's reply was a small thatched cottage, old age, ... and so on. Then someone added the title of [writing capitalist] to Mr. Zhang, and suggested that everyone move into his new house to live.

Mr. Lin Yutang did not stay until the end of the banquet, nodded, said hello, and left alone humorously; while Mr. Xie Liuyi, who loved to write essays, often buried his head in eating vegetables, blew cigarette rings into the sky, and did not talk much. After three rounds of wine and three courses of dishes, the host stood up to speak, humbly and elegantly reporting that this meal was not easy to eat, and there was more to come..., everyone was refreshed and relieved.

Then followed the self-introductions of each person by name, starting with Mr. Li Dachao: [I, Li Dachao, from Guangdong!] Mr. Hu Yuzhi's self-introduction was: [I, Hu Yuzhi, do some irrelevant things in the Oriental Magazine.] [That's an irrelevant thing], a burst of laughter. Mr. Cao Zhongyuan, who played wireless radio tricks, said mischievously and humorously, [I am Cao Cao's Cao, styled Zhongyuan, the second son, and the brother of Cao Mengde.] Then there was another burst of laughter. But fortunately, fortunately, no one was surnamed [Wang] that day.... The last one was Miss Gao, after the [I] word, the voice was so low that it could not be heard. Someone shouted softly: [One more], but it was finally brushed over.

After the introductions, the air was still filled with laughter, talking, and cigarette rings, drinking and eating vegetables. Everyone cheered up again and mobilized fully, and our host, Mr. Li Liewen, was even more like a newly married bride, with a solemn and flushed face, like [Luo Tong killing the four gates], sharing a cup of soup in every pile of busy hands. After the dishes were finished and the dishes were scattered, everyone put down a busy hand, with satisfied smiles on their faces.

After another nod and handshake, the heroes left, and under the lights of the quiet night, everyone went their separate ways home. 乂乂乂乂

Long Novel

Crossroads of the Times and Love (1) 210

— Zhang Ziping

It was more than a month after Lin Haiquan had been living in Professor Zeng Bingyuan's house that he learned that the Japanese wife, who took care of him like a sister and was very happy about his daily life, was his father's friend and also the third wife of Professor Zeng. This was told to him by a classmate named Tang Yaoxing this morning. [So that's how it is. No wonder she is so young. So she is someone's concubine.] Lin Haiquan sat in the rickshaw, feeling that he had undergone a great change in spirit today. As for what kind of change, he himself was inexplicable and could not express it concretely. He only felt that after Tang Yaoxing told him this secret, he felt a sense of disappointment and at the same time discovered a miracle.

[How old is she this year? Not thirty, right? ...I'm afraid she's over thirty. However, she is good at makeup, dressing up like a fashionable female student, but when facing her directly, one can discover the middle-aged features on her face, although very small, but undeniable. ...] Professor Zeng is an expert in economics. After returning from Waseda University in Japan, he lived in the European continent 丨丨Germany and France丨丨 for more than two years before returning to Shanghai in the winter of the year before last. Since he published two or three major works and translations, he has become a celebrity in the publishing world. He is now the head of the economics department of 乂乂 University, a consultant to a certain institution, and a consultant to a certain bank. In the eyes of the party-state dignitaries, he is certainly not worth anything, but in the special zoo 丨丨China's institutions of higher learning丨丨, in the eyes of young people like Lin Haiquan, he is indeed a figure to be envied.

When Haiquan first came to Shanghai from the south, he first visited his father's friend, Zeng Bingyuan. Because Professor Zeng used to teach at a middle school in the south, and he worked with Haiquan's father 丨Haiquan's father was the principal, and he was an English teacher丨.

Before seeing Professor Zeng, Haiquan thought that he must be as old as his father. But after meeting him, it was completely contrary to his imagination. Professor Zeng was still a middle-aged man under forty, and his attitude was as warm and amiable as his appearance, giving Haiquan a very good impression. However, his complexion was a little pale, and there was also a set of black and purple circles around his eyes. This was probably a sign of his hard work and excessive worldly desires.

When Haiquan first arrived in Shanghai, he was unfamiliar with the place, and regarding the issue of residence, he also followed his father's orders and brought it up to ask this father's friend. [Living in a dormitory is also possible. However, ... if you are willing, live here. The houses on the third floor and the garret are empty.] [The garret is a bit cold. The overhanging building is better.]

At that time, Mrs. Zeng, who was just sitting silently on the side listening to her husband and this newly arrived young man talking, suddenly interjected. After she said that, she smiled and looked at Haiquan, and then chirped a string of Japanese to her husband. Haiquan had long known that Professor Zeng's wife was a Japanese woman. But he really did not expect that this Japanese wife's Chinese was so clear.

Before he even passed the university entrance exam, he moved into Professor Zeng's house. [If there is anything inconvenient, just tell me directly. The old nanny in this house is both lazy and disobedient. I'm afraid she won't listen to you. If you have anything, tell me.] When he first moved in, while still tidying up his luggage in the room, Mrs. Zeng 丨丨by Professor Zeng's introduction, her name is Hezi丨丨 walked in with a smile and helped him fold the bedding on the small iron bed. [I'm sorry, I'm sorry, Aunt Zeng, I'm really sorry.]

Seeing Mrs. Hezi so diligently cleaning his bedding, Haiquan just blushed and said sorry to her repeatedly. [It's okay, Mr. Lin. Do you find it strange? But in Japan, this is very common. Women who have been sunbathed will not be young mistresses, only maids. 丨丨Cheap bones.]

Wedding Noodles Feast 211

— Xie Liuyi

Mr. Bo had a baby boy last month. To comfort his wife and celebrate the new budding life, he invited several relatives and friends to hold a simple wedding noodles feast. I wrapped a gift in red paper and wrote a few words on it: [Wishing the future warrior a long life.] This sentence has six more words than the customary [Long life and wealth], although it is a bit fruity, it is the only way to express my feelings. Raising children in this era is really not easy. Not to mention the parents' responsibilities, the children themselves also bear a heavy burden. From the moment they separate from the womb, they are thrown into various environments; and the debts owed by their ancestors must be repaid by this generation. If they don't become warriors, how can they bear the responsibilities of future Chinese people? The French writer Romain Rolland said: [The real warrior dares to face the bleak life.] The children raised now must be asked to be warriors or soldiers, because nothing is more bleak than the life of a weak nation under imperialist oppression. Mr. Bo himself is a warrior, founding a weekly magazine, almost acting as a one-man show. His child should also be a future warrior, so I congratulate his child. Doing things only gets more and more desolate; any silver or gold wedding anniversary celebrations are also more and more cheesy the more they are celebrated. Although the wedding noodles feast is also a traditional custom of patriarchal society, it does not lose its [joy of birth]. It always carries the meaning of celebrating a [new birth]. Holding a wedding noodles feast means that parents are responsible for the newborn child; cultivating their child in all aspects to become a warrior, fighting for themselves and fighting for society and the country. We hope that each generation is better than the last. So, newborn children are worth celebrating. Other than that, the wedding noodles feast has no meaning.

Newborn's Free Talk 212

— Bingying

The Shen Bao has a history of sixty years in the Chinese journalistic world. It would be a great pity if such a long-standing newspaper, which has a deep relationship with the evolution of Chinese society, were to remain stagnant in an era full of contradictions and yet moving forward! In recent days, Mr. Li Liewen invited me to write something for the soon-to-be-reformed [Free Talk]. While I am blessing this newborn [Free Talk] to move forward, I also want to take this opportunity to say a few words casually. I feel that the cultural level of a country and the survival ability of a nation are closely related. Although the May Fourth Movement in China also nurtured some sprouts of new culture, it gradually declined due to the reflection of economic relations. In addition, the drastic devastation in the middle made the culture in the revolutionary process almost take the path of returning to antiquity. In recent years, there seems to have been a sudden change, but in reality, it still shows many different outlines. This is indeed a unique phenomenon in China and the reason why China's cultural movement cannot make long-term progress. This really gives young people a lot of impressions of wandering crossroads. I am unwilling to make excessive demands on this newborn [Free Talk] with purely subjective wishes, but I would like to contribute as much as possible on the themes of grasping the masses that produce China's new cultural life, and I hope that this newborn [Free Talk] can sympathize with it and maintain its balanced progress! Due to the same starting point, I hope that the future [Free Talk] can follow the highest tide of culture to promote the wheel of the times! At least I hope that the works I write myself can have such efforts and gains. Finally, I sincerely wish [Free Talk] to work hard for China's new culture!

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talk

The So-Called Imperial Army Warriors 214

— Buddha

The Japanese laugh at us as [an unorganized country] and as [a country of bandits], and spread this slogan everywhere. Indeed, our warlords are not making progress. In this era, they still have to perform the drama of [internal strife], while bandits and communists take the opportunity to steal and launch attacks. Our country's weaknesses, although not as bad as the Japanese promote, do have places that cannot be glossed over. However, in this world political and economic trend that cannot be stabilized, any country inevitably has events of the same nature occurring, the only difference is the degree. Take Japan as an example. When cabinets rise and fall, the number of important figures assassinated is countless, and cases of communist theft are even more widespread. If we are to speak strictly, in an organized country, and not a country of bandits, the national conditions should naturally not be like this. Today, let me cite one thing to prove it.

[According to the Tokyo Asahi Shimbun yesterday, Nomura, the machine gun platoon leader of the Third Regiment of the Azabu Infantry who was dispatched to Shanghai, returned to Japan from Shanghai. In early May, due to being laid off, on the 18th of this month, he sneaked into the Makihara residence near the Sugamo Prison and robbed it. He was arrested by the Tokyo Metropolitan Police Department. Nomura had previously committed theft. This time he committed robbery again. However, the Metropolitan Police Department considered him an [Imperial Army Warrior] who had been dispatched to Shanghai and, after advising him, released him.]

This is a fact reported by the Tokyo Asahi Shimbun. It can be seen that the personality of the so-called [Imperial Army Warrior] of a civilized country is only like this. Under the principle that good people do not become soldiers, there is no need to demand or blame them further. However, in terms of national law, although our country is an unorganized country, when there was a soldier from a certain company who robbed in Kunshan during the Shanghai battle, our generals immediately dealt with him according to military law and never tolerated him. We will never allow him to violate the law and disrupt discipline because he has contributed to the Anti-Japanese War. Merits should not go unrewarded, and crimes should not go unpunished. This is the great law of the country, and the laws of all countries governed by the rule of law are like this.

Assuming that because they are [Imperial Army Warriors], they are allowed to do whatever they want and no questions are asked, it is directly rewarding warriors and indirectly rewarding bandits. From then on, everyone who has been on the battlefield has an amulet for exemption from crime, and everyone who has served in the military once has the qualification to be a bandit. In this way, theft cases will be endless. Although our country is an unorganized country, we can still recognize the concept of law, while the so-called civilized and organized countries even have special new laws to reward bandits.

Science

Alcohol 215

— Ke

Alcohol is a colorless, light, and volatile liquid. At zero degrees, its specific gravity is equal to 0.8062. It has a pleasant and fast fragrance. Its boiling point is 78 degrees Celsius. It only solidifies at minus 130 degrees Celsius, so it can be used to make thermometers. When burned, it shows a green flame. Its gas mixed with oxygen in the air will explode when burned. The properties of alcohol are roughly as described above. Below, I will talk about its manufacturing method to provide readers with a little common sense.

The manufacturing method of this alcohol is to add brewer's yeast to an extremely dilute sugar solution to ferment it (Fermentation) to produce carbonic acid wine. After 24 hours, take it out and distill it at low temperature to obtain alcohol containing a large amount of water. Then, add dry lime to absorb the water, filter it with cloth, and then distill it at low temperature to obtain relatively pure alcohol, but the limit of its purity is only 98%, and this manufacturing method is for small quantities. As for wanting to make a large quantity, soak barley in water, wait for it to germinate, and when the sprouts grow to three-quarters of the length of the barley, spread it flat for several days, and then dry it with low temperature, crush it with a pestle, then add five-grain flour and boil it, then the starch contained in it will become glucose, then filter it with cloth, let it cool, transfer it to a fermentation barrel, add brewer's yeast to ferment it (the longer the time, the more complete the fermentation). Take it out after an appropriate time, and it will be ordinary beverage wine, which contains about 10% to 50% alcohol, then distill it by distillation. The alcohol obtained before 78 degrees Celsius is alcohol, and the water obtained after 78 degrees Celsius is water, but in actual distillation, a small amount of water is distilled before 78 degrees Celsius, so the alcohol obtained is only 90% to 92%. If you want to refine it further, add quicklime powder to the alcohol to absorb most of the water, filter it, and re-distill it to obtain 98% alcohol, which is the best quality alcohol. The value of this kind of extremely pure alcohol is three or four times that of crude alcohol because the manufacturing loss is too much. To make ordinary cologne, you can use 90% to 92% alcohol, but you must first use bone charcoal to remove its odor to avoid hindrance. If you want to make high-quality cologne, you must use more pure alcohol, so the values of these two are also different. To know whether alcohol contains water or not, you can use the following inspection methods:

(1) Add colorless powder of anhydrous copper sulfate to alcohol. If it turns blue, it is evidence of containing water.

(2) Add kerosene to alcohol. If it contains a large amount of water, it will become cloudy.

(3) Use an alcohol meter to check its specific gravity to know how much water the alcohol contains.

Literature and Art

Feelings on Hearing about the Rampant Bandits 216

— Sun Choucheng

Old Man Tui received a letter from his hometown friend Liu, knowing that the bandits were raising troops outside the city of Hezhou every day. He was deeply anxious and angrily recited this to express his worries. In the countryside of the old home, wild smoke rises. The bandit situation and military reports are both vast and unclear. The lonely city is as big as a dipper, the wind and clouds are evil. The heroes are ambitious, and the fortifications are firm. There is no good place to avoid danger like piled eggs. The aid troops are hopeless, and they cry to the sky in chaos. It takes effort to plan to resolve disputes and difficulties. Who is the outstanding figure like Zhong Lian? The thorny land and thorny sky are too bitter to support. Heroic hot tears are chaotic like silk. Bad clouds press against the battlements, and people are crying. Abusive snow raises dust, and the emperor does not know. Hawks and falcons fly far away, indulging in proud pheasants and rabbits. Jackals and wolves are in power, indulging foxes and raccoons. Scholars emptyly embrace the peace and security strategy. When will they get the axe and handle?

Great Good Day 217

— Ying Dai

For parents, it is a very honorable thing to wait for their children to marry, but the date of the wedding cannot be sloppy. Beforehand, they have to ask a blind fortune teller to calculate the eight characters of the birth date. Otherwise, if unfortunate events happen after the young couple gets married, the parents will feel somewhat sorry for the younger generation. Therefore, for the son's wedding and the daughter's departure, they must ask a blind fortune teller to find a good day. Originally, just in Shanghai, if there were no one coming to calculate the eight characters and look at the good days in the fortune-telling shops that are every three steps or five steps, how would they maintain their lives? However, the skills of these blind fortune tellers are really too great. The dates they see for weddings often cause the happy events of many families to be on the same day. The Zhang family is getting married today, and the Li family is also getting married today, even hundreds or thousands of families are getting married on the same day. I don't understand whether the fates of these many new couples are the same. If they get married on this day, will everyone be infinitely happy in the future!

In fact, to be frank, the blind fortune teller decides on a day, you only need to pay a few dollars, and he will not care about anything else. He is not an insurance company, so how can he guarantee that thousands of marriages will have satisfactory results? Moreover, the good days seen by the blind fortune tellers are nothing more than deceiving people and cheating money. When we get married, we don't ask a blind fortune teller, but because the superstitious power of society is too deep, we have to find a good day in the almanac. As a result, the day you find may be the same as the one the blind fortune teller found for you, so why give these few dollars to the blind fortune teller? However, if everyone is like me, the blind fortune tellers in Shanghai

Page 22

I am afraid that there will be a panic about eating. Yesterday, October 29th of the old calendar was said to be a great good day in the second half of this year. Some blind fortune tellers may have held a blind person's meeting beforehand, so they picked this day as the wedding day for thousands of young men and women. But the panic has occurred. In Shanghai, although there are many restaurants and many hotels, yesterday, they really could not supply so many families getting married. There was too little porridge and too many monks. Those with long hands and fast feet had already booked the auditorium and found the hotel in advance. However, those who lacked experience in handling affairs and were unfamiliar with the situation in Shanghai went to find the auditorium and book the hotel very slowly. I am sorry, ten out of ten families have booked it. Even if you run all over the Chinese and French concessions, you can't find a place. It is said that like the Fuxing Garden on Wuma Road, people go to book the auditorium the year after the wedding. It is originally impossible to book if you are late! Thanks to the blind fortune tellers for fulfilling the wish of many young men and women. Yesterday's moment arrived. In the morning, all the hotels and auditoriums were hung with lights and decorated with red and green. From grandfathers to younger brothers, from grandmothers to modern girls, they all wore new clothes and went to eat wedding banquets. Which one of them didn't have a smiling face. In the streets, cars were flying red flags with [Happy Event at the Palace], picking up and dropping off guests, coming and going like shuttles. Trumpet bands, military bands, red and green, were running so busy. In the taverns, everyone was guessing fingers and shouting orders, making a lot of noise. In the streets, wedding sedan chairs were coming and going everywhere, and the sound of drums and music filled the sky, comparing to the lantern festival; a joyous atmosphere was revealed everywhere, and we cannot but congratulate the blind fortune tellers on their victory and success!

Small Exam 218

— Wo

These past few days, the atmosphere in our noble school has been extremely tense. Why? Is it because the League of Nations is discussing the Manchurian Incident? Is it for helping the Northeast Volunteer Army? No, it's not. It turns out that the school authorities are holding a small exam. Everyone seems to be busy. The usually quiet study room has become unusually lively. Some are reading English textbooks, some are doing physics and chemistry exercises, and some are copying cheat sheets with characters as small as fly legs. At night, after the lights are turned off, candlelight continues to rise. In the morning; around four o'clock, there are many students in the tea room using electric lights to study. The sports field is deserted, and there are no athletes galloping. There are no couples talking in the campus: In short, everything has changed the state of the past. Ten minutes before each exam, the situation in the classroom can be said to be the most tense. Most of the students are holding textbooks to read or look at, as if they are unwilling to give up these last precious ten minutes, but a small number of students! Of course, they are already prepared, chanting English love songs leisurely, or chewing peanuts. During the exam, the classroom is quiet, and you can only hear the sound of the tip of the pen touching the paper and the slight sound of [Hey, pass the question No. ○ over]. The sharp eyes of the invigilator are constantly shooting around, but small pieces of paper are still being passed around from time to time. When he |the invigilator| stands up and walks over, our participating heroes have already sung the song of triumph. After the exam, the winners indeed have smiling faces and sing the song of triumph, but the losers hang their heads and complain, [Mr. A, thank you, please go outside to eat some refreshments], [Mr. B, you are too stingy, why didn't you pass the question No. ○ over?], such sounds are also spreading in the air after the exam.

Progressing Step by Step, Crow's Progress, Opium Tax, Salt Tax, Tax 219

Price 220

— Jia Yu

Temporarily loosening the shackles of life, dragging my dry body, I went back on foot as usual. My stomach sometimes growled with hunger, because my pockets were always empty, so I had to be patient and rush forward. Strange! Tonight is a little different. I thought I would run faster as usual, but it was not as smooth as I imagined. My two feet were a little disobedient, and my stomach was even more uncomfortable. My eyes were a little dizzy when I saw the lights and gradually became blurry. I staggered through the crowd step by step. When I saw an alley near Sima Road, people were pushing and shoving extra busily. A burst of water vapor blew in, mixed with a greasy aroma. My nose felt unusually comfortable, and the saliva dripped down my mouth. My hungry intestines could no longer bear it. I walked in slowly, thinking that I was late coming out to wait for my salary today, no wonder my stomach was growling. Eat! Anyway, there is money in my pocket. I thought to myself and touched the smooth and slippery foreign coins in my pocket. I watched bowls of steaming spare rib noodles being sent over there. The urgency of my empty stomach finally couldn't be resisted, so I sat down. [What would you like to eat, sir?] A waiter wearing a white apron ran over. [Um, a bowl of noodles, spare rib noodles]. I thought that plain noodles were too monotonous and would be looked down upon by the waiter because the diners sitting around me were all working hard to promote the noodle restaurant. [Hey, another bowl, hurry up!] [Okay, sir, coming!] The waiter saw that my promotion ability was not weak and agreed very vigorously. While eating, I thought that the price of these two bowls of noodles, if I took them back, would probably feed my family for a day? Thinking of this, I regretted it a little. It would be enough to eat one bowl to fill my stomach. Why did I have to eat and add it like building a wall? Such expensive noodles, it doesn't matter if you don't eat them and let him be hungry for a while. It may not necessarily starve to death. The more I thought about it, the more I complained. I looked at the uneaten noodle soup and thought that the layer of oil beads on it was probably all made of blood and sweat? Don't waste it, drink it! I picked up the bowl and drank it all in one breath, without even leaving any noodle residue. [Sir, do you want more?] [No more! How much?] [Sir, forty cents! Haha... a hundred cents for a small bill!] I took out a warm foreign coin, gave it to the waiter to find six cents and a few hundred cash, picked it up and left. My two feet also had energy, and my stomach was so full that it was a little inconvenient to breathe. However, today's hard work was only for me to enjoy two bowls of [spare rib noodles] alone!

The Eight Characters Under the Incense Burner 222

— Xu Yu

Old Man Wang is not only rich in property, but his young master is also so handsome and well-dressed, and is currently working in a bank. He has a promising future. Therefore, since the news of the marriage spread, matchmakers have been coming one after another, sending the eight characters of many young ladies to the Wang Mansion for selection. Mrs. Wang received thirty to fifty sets of eight characters and invited many fortune tellers to carefully calculate them one by one. Except for a few ill-fated beauties who were called [bankrupt], [widow], and [offending in-laws] by the blind fortune tellers, there were also a dozen or so girls who were so-called [prosperous and wealthy] and [beneficial to husband and children]. She didn't know which one to marry and was really hesitant. At first, she wanted to marry the one with the richest family among these eight characters, but she felt that in this world of the survival of the fittest, it was not enough to rely on wealth alone without power, and her husband was a businessman who always felt uneasy about selling inferior goods in the store, fearing being inspected and punished. If there was a powerful noble relative, she could rely on his power as a backing, so not only would she not be afraid of secretly smuggling, but she could also pack and transport

Page 23

earn money, so she really wanted to marry an official, but she was a small commoner, although she said republican equality, but after all, she was not a good match and could not hope to climb high. Therefore, she could not reach high and could not reach low, and after expanding and going back, there was no suitable household. Later, she finally found an eight character set with money and power. It was the niece of a bureau chief. Her father was also a businessman who opened a shop, and this Miss Li was virtuous, filial, gentle, knowledgeable, and literate, and had good needlework skills. It was really rare to find such a woman nowadays. However, the old-fashioned Mrs. Wang still followed the old method she knew, which was completely irrational and almost superstitious. She pressed Miss Li's eight characters under the incense burner of the Kitchen God. It is said that [if there are no unexpected changes or unlucky things like bankruptcy within three days, these eight characters are the best, otherwise they are unlucky.] She firmly believes that this is the most appropriate and best way to determine the fate of Miss Li. However, on the evening of the same day, her ancestral white jade cup, which was her most beloved wine cup, was broken by her nephew. She suspected that Miss Li's eight characters were not good and that her fate carried a bankruptcy star. She felt unhappy in her heart. On the third day, she suddenly received a quick letter from her son. She hurriedly asked Mr. Huang next door to read the letter for her. She heard [the bank recently went bankrupt due to losses, her son has lost his job and is about to go home...] and ran angrily to the stove, took out the eight characters pressed under the incense burner, burned them on the fire, and cursed hatefully; [This kind of unlucky eight characters with a bankruptcy star are still sent to harm people!]

Exhaustion 223

— Cheng Xun

Early in the morning, his wife spent an hour and a half dressing up. Finally, she gracefully draped herself in the new coat bought with his month's salary, like a butterfly, and flew out. Inside the room, he was left alone, blankly sitting in a chair.

He was stunned for a good while before slowly turning his head to look at the mess of perfume and powder on the dressing table, and the scattered long and short garments beside the bed. He couldn't help but sigh deeply, stood up, and began to wipe and tidy up everything. He also muttered to himself: [Is my wife, after all, happy?]

They had been married for over a year. Undoubtedly, before the marriage, each of them felt satisfied and content. However, from the perspective of their history after living together, the wife had discovered that he was an ordinary man without wealth or talent. He, on the other hand, bitterly believed that a woman who couldn't manage the household affairs was truly unworthy of being his wife. [Don't you see how considerate Miss Wang's partner is to her! Buying this and arranging that, and her social skills are so active. You only know how to drone on a few lines from books and bite on the end of your pen. You're really an incompetent bookworm. Wouldn't it be embarrassing for me to go out with you?]

[Learn from Mrs. Zhang! She manages the affairs of her home so well. Mr. Zhang is truly happy. Put the effort you spend on makeup and powder into housework! Going out today, leaving tomorrow, what kind of behavior is that?] They had said the above conversation more than once. The wife, as usual, was busy with social engagements and dancing, wearing different leather shoes every day and returning home late at night. She didn't bother to mend his socks, which had large holes, or wash his shirts, which had accumulated into a thick pile. Today, some girlfriend had invited her to dinner, so she took the only ten yuan from his pocket to go out. Poor him, he had planned to use that money to make a robe, but his wife, how could she care about such things!

All the past dissatisfactions and unsympathetic facts were now playing out in his mind like a running horse. He slumped down, looking at the wedding photo of the two of them hanging on the wall, feeling a sense of separation from another world. He couldn't bear it anymore and shouted loudly again: [Is my wife, after all, happy?]

Laughter 224

— Xin Geng

Laughter is a unique human instinct, not found in other animals. For example, dragons roar, tigers howl, apes cry, cranes screech, chickens crow, and dogs bark. They can only produce a kind of uneven sound to express their inner feelings. Only humans, from infancy, can laugh before they can speak. The appearance of laughter is varied, including a gentle smile, a bright smile, a flattering smile, and a hearty laugh. People's false laughter is called ridicule, and mocking people's foolishness is called sarcastic laughter. There are many forms of laughter, too numerous to list. Now, let's discuss them based on the above.

(1) [A gentle smile] After the assassin Zheng Jicheng killed Zhang Zongchang, he was imprisoned in a cell. Someone took a photo of him and published it in the newspapers. His expression was [a gentle smile], smiling because his father's revenge had been avenged, or smiling because he could eliminate harm for the country, and his功 had been established. This is unknowable. This is one kind of laughter. (2) [A bright smile] After the Japanese single-handedly created the Manchurian state, Puyi, covered in sweat, sent envoys and Manchurian girls to Japan to present the national credentials in order to win a bright smile from the Japanese Emperor. This is one kind of laughter. (3) [A flattering smile] After the establishment of the puppet state, Puyi was the puppet leader, Xie Jieshi was the Minister of Foreign Affairs, and the old and unrepentant traitor Zheng Xiaoxu was the Prime Minister. The empty shell was fully displayed, and the situation of Zheng, Xie, and others giving flattering smiles to the Japanese is self-evident. This is also one kind of laughter.

(4) [Hearty laughter] and [Mocking laughter] On the 23rd of the month, at the League of Nations meeting in Geneva, our country's Dr. Gu Weijun refuted the fallacies of the Japanese envoy Matsuoka Yosuke, saying that if boycotting Japanese goods is a disguised form of war, then China welcomes Japan's discrimination against the Chinese, but does not welcome Japan's occupation of the three northeastern provinces. At this point, the whole place burst into laughter. This kind of laughter is mocking the Japanese's delusional attempt to swallow the three northeastern provinces, or mocking China's lack of goods being boycotted by the Japanese. This is one kind of laughter.

Origin of the Shop Assistant Communication Column 225

During this 60th-anniversary celebration, our newspaper, in order to contribute to the business community of this port, has established a circulating library and published a weekend periodical for amateurs. Now, we feel that the social environment of this port is complex, especially for shop assistants and apprentices in various stores and companies, who have more opportunities to contact society due to the nature of their work. Under these circumstances, whether from a social or personal perspective, many difficult problems are bound to arise. However, individual knowledge is ultimately limited, and only by pooling collective wisdom can we achieve the effect of mutual learning. Therefore, we have specially opened a "Shop Assistant Communication" column to welcome everyone to raise various difficult questions. We are willing to do our best to discuss them with everyone sincerely, hoping to find a relatively proper and satisfactory solution. If we encounter topics that are beyond our ability to answer, we will invite experts to explain them. Shop Assistant Communication Column Regulations (1) Purpose of Communication: The purpose of this column is to pool collective wisdom, explain difficult problems, learn from each other, and enhance the happiness of life. (2) Target Audience: The target audience of this column is limited to shop assistants and apprentices in terms of people, and limited to this port in terms of location. (3) Content of Communication: All questions about personal daily life, such as: (1) Occupation, (2) Moral and academic cultivation, (3) Entertainment and sports, (4) Marriage, etc., as well as other questions related to the country and society, are welcome. If the content of the question is too profound and beyond the ability of this column, it can also be introduced to this newspaper's [Reader Advisory] to answer it on our behalf.

(4) Method of Letter Submission: (1) The letter must clearly state the name, age, native place, occupation, and detailed mailing address; the same information must be provided in subsequent letters. (2) The writing style of the letter is not limited, but it should be simple and easy to understand, and it must be written clearly. (3) Please write "Shen Bao Newspaper, This Port Supplement, Shop Assistant Communication Column" on the envelope; if a reply is needed, please attach a two-cent stamp. (4) Communicators must cut out the special stamp issued by this column and paste it on the upper left corner of the letter; letters without the stamp will not be answered. (5) Processing Method After Receiving Letters: (1) Any questions discussed that this newspaper deems to have value in contributing to the public may be disclosed in the newspaper. (2) In order to respect the opinions of the communicator, if the letter states that the writer does not want their name disclosed or requires a private response, it will be handled accordingly. (3) If the communicator hopes to disclose the letter in the newspaper, but the length is too long to be fully disclosed, the main points will be published. In addition, if the content of the question is complex and requires careful study, resulting in a delayed response or disclosure, readers are requested to understand. (4) When there is a backlog of letters, answers will be given in the order in which they were received, and any delays are requested to be understood.

Fiction

The Sympathizer 226

— Zhang Henshui

(1) Tian The weather in the south of the Yangtze River after May is already unbearably hot. However, the villagers in the countryside are busy harvesting barley and starting to plant rice. The plants and trees are also as excited as the farmers, vigorously growing outwards. The entire plain is covered with paddy fields. The rice seedlings have pierced the surface of the water in the fields and are already more than a foot long. If people look at the plain from a distance, they will see green everywhere. The plain is surrounded by green trees on all sides, except for the distant green mountains. This is not because the villagers planted trees to surround the paddy fields. Because the trees scattered in various places on the plain, regardless of whether they are dense or sparse, no matter where you look, you always feel that you are standing in a suitable location. Beyond the trees all around, it is the green sky like a dome, and you feel that the trees are linked together. It is noon, and a few white clouds float in the sky, further embellishing the green fields and making them bright and open. Occasionally, large white egrets fly out of the green paddy fields, which is even more poetic. Perhaps some people have appreciated the beauty of this great nature. Suddenly, a burst of singing rises from the green fields. He sings: Looking from afar, oh elder sister, walking all the way, applying half a catty of powder on your face. Looking up close, you look like a hanging ghost. Looking from afar, you look like a fox spirit, oh fox spirit! Almost scared the soul out of this talented brother, oh. The person seemed to be very happy singing. After finishing one song, he sang another song: The sun sets down, the birds in the pond, the sister washing in the room... [Hey! Second brother! Stop singing. There's a woman walking past on the road over there.] [What does it matter? A song can't be sung without a lover or sister.] A farmer with a weeding sickle in his hand was weeding in the field. A college student who had returned to his hometown from the city was walking with his hands behind his back on the bank of the field and talking to him. The farmer was called Wang Laoer, and the student was Meng Guobao. They were from the same village, but Meng Guobao had always studied in the provincial capital and rarely returned to his hometown. Even recently, he hadn't returned for three years. Because he was studying social science, he felt that China's rural economy had collapsed in recent years, so he deliberately went to the countryside to investigate the conditions of the rural society. As a child is fond of sweets all the year round, so the time was idle and he went to the field to see the work of the farmers. He heard Wang Laoer singing a song that was almost indecent, so he interrupted his singing and said with a smile, "Although a song can't be sung without a lover or sister, there are many things to say about lovers and sisters. Why do you have to sing such an unpleasant one?" Laoer's sickle scraped back and forth in the mud, splashing the water, and he lowered his head, panting and laughing, "Nine out of ten songs are from Dong, and one that's not from Dong is still proper. Isn't everyone singing like that? If women hear it, they hear it. Anyway, it's just that kind of thing." Meng Guobao saw that the small bamboo hat he was wearing couldn't cover the back of his neck, but he draped a long blue cloth over his shoulders to block the strong sunlight. He exposed a large section of his back, and his skin was tanned yellow and black, and he even smeared it with a layer of grease, making it look almost like cowhide. His upper body had been tempered and he was not wearing clothes. Even his lower body, a pair of blue cloth trousers, had the trouser legs rolled up and flattened his leg grooves. If he removed that draped blue cloth, he would be close to a person from the primitive era who was wearing leaves.
